# Engine log

The dated narrative for material engine changes ŌĆö the third layer of the four-layer trace system named in [ADR 0036](adr/0036-expression-contract-for-inward-documents.md) (ADRs / engine log / MemPalace `decision`-tagged drawers / git history). The "engine" is the AI build apparatus the user and Claude run together to construct Paideia: session lifecycle, validators, hooks, MemPalace integration, operations docs, ADRs about how the AI works. This file is **not** Paideia's product release log; that role is reserved for [`CHANGELOG.md`](CHANGELOG.md), which carries a reserved-stub preamble until Phase 9 release prep authors the v1.0.0 entry. Per [ADR 0037](adr/0037-engine-product-wall-and-changelog-rename.md), the reservation is explicit at the filename layer so a future contributor or session walking up cold does not re-create the file under conventional Keep-a-Changelog assumptions.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.1.0/) with project-specific calibration: changes are scoped to **state-of-record** engine artifacts (design docs, schemas, seed graph migrations, build_plan, ADRs, OPERATIONS-equivalent docs, top-level project files). Application code (React, API endpoints, UI) is **git-only** ŌĆö its history lives in the commit log, not here.

This project does not yet follow [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/) ŌĆö versions are milestones (`0.0.x` for foundation; `0.1.0` at foundation close; later versions track product readiness).

---

## [Unreleased]

### Added (S-0093 ŌĆö issue close-out campaign C4: MemPalace effectiveness pair, Issues #38 + #39)

- **New tool [`engine/tools/mempalace_boot_search.py`](tools/mempalace_boot_search.py)** ŌĆö boot-time orchestrator per [ADR 0056](adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md) S-0093 amendment, closes [Issue #38](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/38). Three formulations of the work-item phrase (literal / conceptual / adjacent) via `mempalace.mcp_server.tool_search` with `min_similarity=0.6`. Idempotent `## Prior context (MemPalace boot search)` section in `engine/session/current_plan.md`. JSONL telemetry shim into `engine/session/current_mempalace.jsonl` so `search_calls` increments correctly (orchestrator imports `tool_search` directly, bypassing the PostToolUse hook). Mode-aware work-item resolution: `current.json.working_on` ŌåÆ `auto_target.json` first pending task `name` (routine) ŌåÆ `STATE.md` "Next session work item" block. Substrate-unreachable paths emit a notice + skip the shim.
- **New tool [`engine/tools/scan_mempalace_citations.py`](tools/scan_mempalace_citations.py)** ŌĆö sibling shutdown scanner per ADR 0056 S-0093 amendment, closes [Issue #39](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/39). Runs at shutdown step 8b (after diary write + outcome_summary fill). Scans three sources for citation patterns: `outcome_summary`, today's diary entry (via `tool_diary_read(agent_name="claude", last_n=3)` matched on date), git commit messages from `git log <eager-claim-sha>..HEAD --format=%B`. Three regex patterns: `DRAWER_ID_PATTERN` (`drawer_<wing>_<hash>`), `SESSION_ARCHIVE_PATTERN` (`per/from/at/in/see S-NNNN` and `S-NNNN's <noun>`), `TAG_NAMED_PATTERN` (`per pushback/lesson/decision drawer`). Per-source dedup; cross-source sums. Writes nested `mempalace_citations` block under existing `mempalace_activity` field ŌĆö rides the existing `REQUIRED_ARCHIVE_FIELDS` row in `audit_archive_structured_fields.py` per Layer 4 parameterization, no new audit row.
- **New soft-warn category `mempalace_zero_citations_after_search`** in [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) `validate_mempalace_adoption()`. Fires when `mempalace_activity.search_calls > 0 AND mempalace_activity.mempalace_citations.total == 0` ŌĆö closed-loop check that retrieved drawers actually inform authored artifacts. Gated on session id Ōēź S-0093 (pre-S-0093 archives lack the citations block by design and would fire spuriously). Body cites the S-0093 amendment + ADR 0042 lifecycle. Validator check count rises 17 ŌåÆ 18.
- **27 new pytests** in [`engine/tools/test_mempalace_boot_search.py`](tools/test_mempalace_boot_search.py) ŌĆö formulation generation determinism, similarity-filter behavior, current_plan.md section write/upsert idempotency, JSONL telemetry shim shape, empty-result handling, substrate-unreachable handling, mode resolution.
- **27 new pytests** in [`engine/tools/test_scan_mempalace_citations.py`](tools/test_scan_mempalace_citations.py) ŌĆö pattern coverage (three patterns ├Ś multiple match shapes), per-source dedup + cross-source sum, multi-source aggregation, empty-source handling, idempotency, edge cases (URL false-positive avoidance, non-string outcome_summary, missing diary).
- **6 new pytests** in [`engine/tools/test_validate_mempalace_adoption.py`](tools/test_validate_mempalace_adoption.py) under `TestZeroCitationsAfterSearch` ŌĆö search-with-zero-citations fires, no-search-no-citations vacuous, search-with-citations no fire, missing block defensive, malformed block defensive, body names search_calls.
- **923 engine/tools tests pass; mypy --strict + ruff check + ruff format clean** across all touched files.

- **[ADR 0056](adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md) in-place amendment** ŌĆö single S-0093 block titled "Amendment ŌĆö S-0093 (boot-search effectiveness + drawer-citation telemetry)" covering both Issues #38 and #39. Records: Issue #38 mechanism (orchestrator + telemetry shim + section write), Issue #39 mechanism (scanner + nested citations block + new soft-warn), cross-mode coverage table (engine + routine identical), cascade analysis (additive only ŌĆö no supersession; existing categories unchanged). Pattern matches the existing four amendment blocks (S-0087, S-0089, S-0090, S-0091). Decision drawer captured at `paideia/decisions` per the two-layer-decision-recording rule (drawer ID `drawer_paideia_decisions_b583b22e17599be2d621a183`).
- **Layer 1 ops doc updates** (per ADR 0044 doc-then-skill flow): `engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md` "Mechanical adoption checks" gains two new subsections (boot-search effectiveness orchestrator, drawer-citation telemetry); `session-build-lifecycle.md` step 3 gains orchestrator invocation prose; `routine-mode-operations.md` step 5.5 replaced with orchestrator invocation; step 6 plan-authoring instructions reference the orchestrator's output section; `session-shutdown-sequence.md` adds new step 8b (citation scan); `soft-warn-lifecycle.md` mentions new category alongside post-S-0078 categories; `tools-validate-interpretation.md` registers new soft-warn entry between `retired_surface_used` and `hnsw_divergence` with interpretation + tuning paths.

### Added (S-0092 ŌĆö issue close-out campaign C3: historical full-encoded-path wings deep cleanup)

- **`engine/tools/prune_mempalace.py` `--audit-historical-paths --apply` path** wired (was previously report-only since S-0088). Closes [Issue #41](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/41) ŌĆö 9 historical wings holding 37,634 inaccessible drawers across `mempalace_drawers` plus 67 closet entries in `mempalace_closets`. Apply path now fans deletes out by chromadb collection via the new helper `fetch_uuids_by_collection` (joins `embeddings` -> `segments` -> `collections`) ŌĆö discovered as a load-bearing fix during the S-0092 first apply against live, where the original drawer-only delete left 67 closet rows surviving (closets carry the same `-Users-...` wing tag as their grouped drawers; `collection.delete` is collection-scoped).
- **New helper `fetch_uuids_by_collection`** in `prune_mempalace.py` ŌĆö returns `dict[collection_name, list[uuid]]` so the apply path can target each collection explicitly. The two known target collections (`mempalace_drawers`, `mempalace_closets`) are deleted from; any other collection surfaces as a WARN note rather than a silent miss. `delete_drawers_by_uuid` gained an optional `collection` parameter (default `mempalace_drawers`) so the orphan-wings + mined-ops-docs callers stay backward-compatible.
- **New audit report** at [`engine/docs/audits/historical-wings-signal-probe-S-0092.md`](docs/audits/historical-wings-signal-probe-S-0092.md). Two-pass direct-sqlite signal probe across all 37,634 historical-wing drawers: aggregate query verified zero non-empty `tag`, zero non-empty `type`, all `added_by=mempalace`, all `room=general` ŌĆö confirming the S-0086 R3 #40C "Recommend retire" hypothesis with a definitive count rather than extrapolation. Cleared the Phase 1 halt-and-escalate trigger for the bulk-delete.
- **Pre-flight backups** at `~/.mempalace/palace.S-0092-pre-c3` (550M, captured the full 47,298-drawer pre-cleanup state) and `~/.mempalace/palace.S-0092-pre-closet-cleanup` (captured the post-drawer-delete pre-closet-cleanup state). Both retained on-disk per the S-0084 + S-0088 backup discipline; rollback via atomic-rename swap if anomalies surface in subsequent sessions.
- 8 new pytests in [`engine/tools/test_prune_mempalace.py`](tools/test_prune_mempalace.py) ŌĆö covers dry-run shape, apply-path deletion across both collections (canonical wings preserved), idempotency, the new helper enumerator, the new `fetch_uuids_by_collection` helper (multi-collection bucketing + empty-input short-circuit), CLI backup-dir gate, CLI happy path. 33 tests in the file; mypy --strict + ruff check + ruff format clean.
- [`engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`](operations/mempalace-operations.md) Prune procedure section: the historical-paths mode is now described as full apply-path-capable (was "report-only" pre-S-0092); classifier table extended with the historical-paths apply contract; example invocations include the historical-paths apply form. The S-0086 cross-reference + the closet-collection discovery are both named.

### Changed (S-0092 ŌĆö palace footprint after deep cleanup)

- **MemPalace footprint dropped 79.2%** from 47,298 -> 9,819 drawers (delta -37,479). Wing count dropped from 13 to 7 (paideia, wing_paideia, wing_claude, sessions, plus three short-form per-worktree wings: wing_4840fe, wing_236026, wing_83d301). All 9 historical full-encoded-path wings cleared end-to-end across both `mempalace_drawers` and `mempalace_closets`. The `mempalace_wing_count_growth` soft-warn (post-S-0088 informational threshold 60) sits comfortably below threshold post-cleanup.

### Changed (S-0091 ŌĆö close the no-token-no-diary hard-fail in routine mode + LOUD body uniformity + pending-diary index)

- **New soft-warn category `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_routine`** in [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) ŌĆö fires when `mempalace_activity.diary_write_calls == 0` AND `outcome_summary` lacks the acknowledgement token AND `mode == "routine"`. Replaces the engine-mode-only `mempalace_diary_write_skipped` HARD-FAIL for routine sessions. Engine retains the hard-fail (asymmetry justified by the unattended-vs-interactive difference: engine has an immediate fix path; routine cannot be killed by intermittent MCP per user directive *"I don't want any hard failures of mempalace MCP access because that holds up the whole line of routine sessions"*). LOUD body: `ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ ROUTINE DIARY DEFERRED ŌĆö DO NOT BURY THIS`. Side effect: appends to a new `engine/session/diary_pending_index.json`.
- **LOUD body uniformly across modes** for the four substrate-availability soft-warns (`mempalace_substrate_at_close`, `mempalace_diary_write_acknowledged_skip`, `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_substrate_intermittent`, `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_routine`). Drops the S-0089/S-0090 engine/routine LOUD-vs-standard differentiation. Per user pushback at S-0090 close: *"I have to know that happened clearly in the session text so that when I review I can reconnect MCP and tell the session to do their diary entry later."* Archive review is the routine-side visibility surface; the ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ prefix costs nothing extra in routine archives while serving the "clearly in session text" requirement directly. `_build_substrate_unavailable_body` lost its `mode` parameter.
- **New pending-diary index** at [`engine/session/diary_pending_index.json`](session/diary_pending_index.json). Schema `{schema_version: 1, pending: [{session_id, closed_ts, reason, outcome_summary_excerpt, archive_path}]}`. Mutable, committed to git. New helper `_append_to_diary_pending_index` in `validate.py` is idempotent against re-runs in a single session and degrades gracefully (logs to stderr, does not crash) when the index is missing or malformed. Operational allowlist entry in [`engine/tools/check_routine_scope.py`](tools/check_routine_scope.py) so routine-mode commits can write to it regardless of the active task's `scope_lock.allowed_paths`.
- **Boot-time pending-diary surface** in [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh). Reads the index; emits a LOUD attention block listing the count + session IDs when non-empty. Appears at every boot until processed. Block points at the recovery procedure documentation.
- **Recovery procedure documented** in [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) ŌĆö new "Deferred diary recovery" section. Manual procedure: reconnect MCP, open interactive session, read each pending archive, author a diary entry from the structured fields (`outcome_summary` + `work_done` + `mempalace_activity`), call `mempalace_diary_write`, remove the index entry. No new slash command (deliberate scope limit).
- 8 new pytest cases in [`engine/tools/test_validate_mempalace_adoption.py`](tools/test_validate_mempalace_adoption.py) under `TestRoutineProtectionS0091` ŌĆö covers routine soft-warn (no hard-fail), LOUD body, index append, idempotency, missing-index graceful, malformed-index graceful, token-present-routine-doesn't-fire-skipped-routine, diary-written-routine-doesn't-touch-index. 5 existing `TestSubstrateTokenTightening` tests updated for LOUD-uniform body assertions: `test_token_substrate_intermittent_routine_standard_body` ŌåÆ `..._routine_loud_body`; `test_routine_session_acknowledged_skip_uses_standard_body` ŌåÆ `..._uses_loud_body`; `test_substrate_at_close_routine_standard_body` ŌåÆ `..._routine_loud_body`; `test_no_diary_no_token_substrate_alive_hard_fails` ŌåÆ `test_engine_no_diary_no_token_substrate_alive_hard_fails` (engine-only assertion). 37 tests in the file; 855 tests in `engine/tools/`; all pass. mypy --strict clean.
- [`engine/adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md`](adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md) ŌĆö **third Decision-history entry** (Amendment ŌĆö S-0091) recording the routine-protection refinement. Cross-references the user pushback quote, the plan file, and the implementation files. Coverage table contrasts engine vs. routine across all five mempalace-availability paths post-S-0091.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) ŌĆö `mempalace_diary_write_skipped` entry rewritten as engine-mode-only; new `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_routine` entry; the three substrate-availability soft-warn entries (`substrate_intermittent`, `acknowledged_skip`, `substrate_at_close`) updated to document the uniformly-LOUD body shape post-S-0091.
- [`engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`](operations/mempalace-operations.md) ŌĆö adoption-checks table extended with the new `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_routine` row plus all four substrate-availability rows; **Severity rationale** paragraph rewritten to articulate the engine-vs-routine asymmetry; **Token contract** paragraph extended with the S-0091 layer (no-token routine path doesn't need the token; engine retains the original hard-fail behavior).
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) ŌĆö `outcome_summary_soft_warns` known-categories block extended with the five mempalace-availability soft-warn keys; the trailing paragraph documents the new `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_routine` category and its side effect on `diary_pending_index.json`.

### Changed (S-0090 ŌĆö routine-protection refinement of S-0089's MCP-availability tightening)

- **`mempalace_diary_write_skipped_invalid_token` HARD-FAIL converted to `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_substrate_intermittent` SOFT-WARN** in `validate.py --final-check`. Per user clarification at S-0089 close: *"It's easy for me to fix the MCP connection issue. Seems that Claude Desktop has to be periodically rebooted to keep that working. I just need to know when it happens. I don't want that to kill routine sessions running overnight or while I'm AFK though."* S-0089's hard-fail blocked the close when substrate was alive but token was present ŌĆö the routine-killing scenario the user rules out. S-0090 converts to mode-aware soft-warn: engine LOUD ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ "MCP INTERMITTENT ŌĆö DO NOT BURY THIS"; routine standard one-line. Visibility preserved (engine operator sees the contradiction; routine archive review surfaces the warn); routines close cleanly even on intermittent MCP. The S-0087/S-0088 burial pattern remains structurally hard to repeat because the LOUD body for engine sessions surfaces the substrate-alive + token-present contradiction explicitly.
- 2 new pytest cases in [`engine/tools/test_validate_mempalace_adoption.py`](tools/test_validate_mempalace_adoption.py) (`test_token_substrate_intermittent_engine_loud_soft_warn` + `test_token_substrate_intermittent_routine_standard_body`) replace the prior `test_token_invalid_when_substrate_alive`. 29 tests in the file; all pass.
- [`engine/adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md`](adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md) ŌĆö **Consequences amendment** at S-0090 recording the routine-protection refinement. Cross-references the user clarification quote.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) ŌĆö `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_invalid_token` hard-fail entry removed; new `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_substrate_intermittent` soft-warn entry with mode-aware body documentation; `mempalace_diary_write_acknowledged_skip` entry's stale "token invalidated" sentence corrected to reflect S-0090's always-soft-warn-closure contract.
- [`engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`](operations/mempalace-operations.md) ŌĆö **Mechanical adoption checks** section's token-contract paragraph rewritten to document the S-0089 + S-0090 layered contract (token always downgrades to soft-warn; category depends on substrate state at close).

### Added (S-0089 ŌĆö MCP-availability boot/close warning surfaces + escape-hatch token tightening)

- **Boot-time MCP-availability probe** in [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) ŌĆö runs `mempalace status` at every session boot; LOUD attention block when CLI is missing OR substrate fails. Same surface treatment as ADR 0045's hard-broken probe findings. Mode-uniform at boot (hook fires before `/start-engine` or `/start-routine`); LOUD shape ensures the user sees it at the earliest possible moment regardless of session type.
- **Close-time substrate probe** in `validate.py --final-check` via new helper `_check_mempalace_substrate_alive()`. Uses `python3 -m mempalace status` to bypass PATH issues (mirrors the existing ruff/mypy/pytest invocation pattern). New soft-warn category `mempalace_substrate_at_close` fires when substrate is unreachable, independent of diary-write state. **Mode-aware body:** engine sessions get LOUD ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ "DO NOT BURY THIS" prefix; routine sessions get a one-line standard body. Surfaces broken substrate as its own signal so the user sees it at every close, not only when the acknowledgement token is used.
- **New hard-fail category `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_invalid_token`** ŌĆö fires when the `mempalace_unavailable_acknowledged:` token is present in `outcome_summary` BUT `mempalace status` succeeds at close-time. The token claims substrate unavailable; reality contradicts; the diary skip is the AI burying a real failure (the S-0087 + S-0088 burial pattern). Blocks the close ŌĆö forces the AI to either invoke `mempalace_diary_write` immediately (since MCP is live) or investigate the upstream MCP-load timing issue.
- 13 new pytest cases in [`engine/tools/test_validate_mempalace_adoption.py`](tools/test_validate_mempalace_adoption.py) covering: token-invalid-when-substrate-alive (hard-fail), token-valid-when-substrate-down (soft-warn), engine-LOUD-body, routine-standard-body, substrate-at-close fires independently of diary state, substrate-at-close silent when alive but check still registered, and the helper's subprocess-run mocking branches (zero exit, nonzero, missing CLI, timeout, `python3 -m mempalace` form). All 28 tests in the file pass.

### Changed (S-0089 ŌĆö operations docs absorb the MCP-availability mechanism)

- [`engine/adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md`](adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md) ŌĆö **Consequences amendment** recording the S-0089 tightening: boot probe + close probe + token-validity tightening + LOUD body for engine sessions. Names the burial pattern (S-0087 + S-0088 archives both used the token while substrate was actually live) and the user pushback that named the gap. Pattern: in-place amendment, no supersession.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) ŌĆö registers the new `mempalace_diary_write_skipped_invalid_token` hard-fail category; expands `mempalace_diary_write_acknowledged_skip` documentation with the mode-aware LOUD/standard body distinction; new `mempalace_substrate_at_close` soft-warn entry.
- [`engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`](operations/mempalace-operations.md) ŌĆö **Maintenance probes** section gains the MCP-availability probe entry (paired with the existing HNSW divergence detection); **Mechanical adoption checks** section's acknowledgement-token escape-hatch paragraph extended with the S-0089 tightening rule.

### Added (S-0088 ŌĆö Issue close-out campaign session C2: MemPalace cleanup execution + boot-time guardrails)

- [`engine/tools/prune_mempalace.py`](tools/prune_mempalace.py) ŌĆö **MemPalace prune tool** per [Issue #40](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/40). Three modes: `--audit-mined-ops-docs` (delete S-0002-mined drawers in `paideia/general` + `paideia/operations`), `--audit-orphan-wings` (delete `wing_<6-hex>` per-worktree orphans), `--audit-historical-paths` (report-only enumeration; deletion deferred to C3 / S-0089 per [Issue #41](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/41)). Default dry-run; `--apply` mutates with mandatory `--backup-dir` (mirrors the [`mempalace_rebuild_hnsw.py`](tools/mempalace_rebuild_hnsw.py) Phase 0 backup discipline from S-0084). Direct chromadb `collection.delete(ids=...)`; sqlite-backed metadata enumeration (~2 s on 47 K-drawer palace).
- [`engine/tools/test_prune_mempalace.py`](tools/test_prune_mempalace.py) ŌĆö coverage for classifier patterns (orphan-wing regex, historical-full-path regex, mined `added_by` exact match), each audit mode (dry-run + apply), CLI-level error paths (missing palace, missing backup-dir, failing backup), and post-apply state verification (canonical wings preserved, mined drawers deleted, `claude-s0002-manual` curated drawers preserved).
- **`mempalace_wing_count_growth` soft-warn** in [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) per [Issue #46](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/46). Parses `[probe-palace] wings: N (total)` from `probe_palace.py` extension; emits soft-warn at Ōēź informational threshold (Tier 1) or LOUD-attention soft-warn at Ōēź loud threshold (Tier 2). Body cross-references Issues #1, #2, #40, #41 and discipline rule that thresholds may only be raised AFTER cleanup batch lands. Validator `check_count` rises 17 ŌåÆ 18.
- **Wing-count probe extension** in [`engine/tools/probe_palace.py`](tools/probe_palace.py) ŌĆö adds `_count_wings()` that queries `chroma.sqlite3`'s `embedding_metadata` table directly (`COUNT(DISTINCT string_value) WHERE key='wing'`) and emits the canonical `[probe-palace] wings: N (total)` line on the healthy path. ChromaDB stores all drawers in two collections (`mempalace_drawers` + `mempalace_closets`) with `wing` carried as metadata, so `len(client.list_collections())` is structurally always 2 ŌĆö distinct-wing query is the only accurate accumulation surface.
- **Audit-trail boot surface** in [`engine/tools/scan_issue_backlog.py`](tools/scan_issue_backlog.py) per [Issue #47](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/47). Emits a second FYI line `[session-start] Active health-check audits: N (M open recommendations).` followed by indented audit-report paths, when `health-check-finding`-labeled Issues are present. Audit cross-references extracted via the `engine/docs/audits/<file>.md` regex (URL and bare-relative-path forms). Issues with the label but no detectable audit ref still count toward M.
- **`wing_count_growth_thresholds` block** in [`engine/session/register_state.json`](session/register_state.json) ŌĆö `{informational: 60, loud: 100}` plus `_history` companion mirroring the `health_check_cadence_history` shape. Threshold reader silently falls back to defaults on absent / malformed config; bootstrap entry attributes the values to S-0088 / Issue #46.

### Changed (S-0088 ŌĆö operations docs absorb the C2 mechanism additions)

- [`engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`](operations/mempalace-operations.md) ŌĆö new **Maintenance probes** section grouping HNSW divergence detection with the new wing-count probe; new **Prune procedure** section documenting `prune_mempalace.py` invocations + classifier signals (DELETE / PRESERVE table) + post-prune verification + tag-weighted retention policy.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) ŌĆö registers the `mempalace_wing_count_growth` category alongside the existing `mempalace_hnsw_divergence` template (trigger one-liner + threshold-tier explanation + recovery path naming `prune_mempalace.py`).
- [`engine/operations/issue-discipline.md`](operations/issue-discipline.md) ŌĆö `Boot-time backlog visibility` section gains a new bullet documenting the audit-trail line: trigger condition, format, lineage-preservation intent.

### Removed (S-0088 ŌĆö MemPalace prune execution)

- **414 mined ops-doc drawers** in `paideia/general` + `paideia/operations` deleted via `prune_mempalace.py --audit-mined-ops-docs --apply`. Source files (`MISSION.md`, `learner-model.md`, `tensions.md`, `architecture.md`, `pedagogy.md`, etc.) already in version control; reading via `Read` is more efficient than retrieval. Pre-prune backup at `~/.mempalace/palace.S-0088-pre-prune`.
- **79 orphan-wing drawers across 51 `wing_<6-hex>` wings** deleted via `prune_mempalace.py --audit-orphan-wings --apply`. Auto-capture artifacts of the upstream wing-naming bug per [Issue #1](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/1) / [Issue #2](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/2); all `type=diary_entry` with no `decision`/`pushback`/`lesson` markers (audit's "Recommend retire" verdict). Intermediate post-mined backup at `~/.mempalace/palace.S-0088-post-mined`.
- **Net effect:** 493 drawers removed (47,683 ŌåÆ 47,190). Wing count 64 ŌåÆ 13. New `mempalace_wing_count_growth` soft-warn fired pre-prune (64 > informational threshold of 60), cleared post-prune (13 < 60). `mempalace repair-status` post-prune reports status OK (HNSW 47,204 / SQLite 47,072 within flush-lag tolerance). Closes [Issue #40](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/40) parts A and B; part C (40K+ historical full-encoded-path drawers across 9 wings) remains C3 / S-0089 scope per [Issue #41](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/41).

### Added (S-0086 ŌĆö Issue close-out campaign session S-D: MemPalace adversarial review)

- [`engine/docs/audits/mempalace-adversarial-review-S-0086.md`](docs/audits/mempalace-adversarial-review-S-0086.md) ŌĆö **adversarial review of MemPalace per [Issue #35](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/35).** First concrete application of [ADR 0057](adr/0057-adversarial-stance-for-health-check-audits.md)'s adversarial-stance posture (the formal first-exercise of ADR 0057 remains the cadence-fired audit at S-0087). **Verdict: scale back.** The audit weighs both fit-historically AND fit-to-CONTINUE (per user direction during plan-mode review): historical evidence (12 of 12 pre-S-0078 sessions S-0066ŌåÆS-0077 had zero MemPalace calls; ADR 0056 mechanically forced Ōēź1 call/session post-S-0078) underdetermines forward fit because the forward-fit map is decisive ŌĆö Phase 6 self-correction, Phase 7 teaching layer, Phase DEC.1 (OQ-DEC1-A/B/C/D), OQ-CONTEXT-COMPRESSION, and OQ-PEDAGOGY-INFERENCE-LOCUS all specify Postgres + pgvector + ephemeral in-session summarization with **zero MemPalace dependency in product runtime**, while ADR 0057's cadence-audit `pushback`/`lesson` substrate, ADR 0051's routine-mode boot diary read, two-layer decision recording, and engine-side cross-session pattern detection are **load-bearing forward**. The load-bearing core (decisions room: 72 drawers tracking 58 ADRs with substantive content; lessons: 117 concrete failure-mode recoveries; problems: 291 verbatim pushback moments; diary: 160 entries; well-targeted boot search returning 6/6 substantive content on substantive queries; hooks + probe per ADR 0045 + S-0084) earns its weight; the dead-weight perimeter (KG / tunnels / AAAK-for-project / 88 mined ops-doc drawers / 50+ orphaned per-worktree wings / 40K+ inaccessible historical full-encoded-path wings / `mempalace_status` protocol-message overhead) does not. Per ADR 0057 element 1 (user-buffered execution), the audit produces 8 numbered recommendations (R1ŌĆōR8: implement Issues #38/#39/#40 with audit-specified scope expansion; small-scope ADR 0056 amendment recording the verdict; ops-doc and tagging-conventions updates) ŌĆö execution work lands downstream after user adjudication. Cold-context probe target: ADR 0048 (random-pick from `find engine/operations engine/adr docs/health-checks engine/build_readiness -name '*.md' -type f`); read healthy with no drift.

### Added (S-0085 ŌĆö Issue close-out campaign session S-C: health-check audit posture overhaul)

- [ADR 0057](adr/0057-adversarial-stance-for-health-check-audits.md) ŌĆö **adversarial stance for project health-check audits.** Sibling to [ADR 0040](adr/0040-build-readiness-gate-before-substantive-build-sessions.md) (gate-side adversarial reconnaissance) at the cadence-audit endpoint. Closes [Issue #30](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/30) (adversarial-stance posture, structurally upstream of #28 and #36), [Issue #28](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/28) (freshness probes per external system; stats-as-proxy-for-function anti-pattern named), [Issue #36](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/36) (pushback/lesson drawer content reading + clustering at audit time). Five contract elements: (1) **user-buffered execution** ŌĆö audit findings + guidance suggestions surfaced *before* any retire/convert/replace action; user adjudicates; downstream sessions execute via Issues per ADR 0048 (added per user pushback during plan-mode review: "The health checks adversarial stance needs to be buffered by reporting its findings and guidance suggestions to me before taking action"); (2) **posture inversion** ŌĆö adversarial prompt-question rewrites for Fit/Gaps/Infrastructure-without-function/Bloat with recommendation-shape dispositions (`recommend retire / recommend convert / recommend preserve-with-affirmative-case`); (3) **stats-as-proxy-for-function** named anti-pattern ŌĆö every system reference rests on a content probe run during the audit, not citations of cached stats; (4) **required output Ōēź1 affirmative retire-candidate-recommendation** (or adversarially-scrutinized explicit "no candidates" subsection); (5) **cold-context probe per audit** ŌĆö read Ōēź1 randomly-selected artifact as if no project context. First-exercise gate per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md); the cadence-fired audit at S-0087 is the first exercise.
- "Adversarial stance" section in [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) carrying the user-buffered execution principle, stats-as-proxy anti-pattern, posture inversion principle, cold-context probe specification.
- "Mechanical inputs and freshness probes" section in [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) (renamed from "Mechanical inputs"). Per-system freshness-probe inventory ŌĆö MemPalace search-recall content quality, validator soft-warn acted-on rate (`git log --grep` per persistent category vs archive `outcome_summary_soft_warns` deltas), Supabase migration empirical postcondition, hook-log success-exit verification, register-content capture rate. Documents `health_check.py`'s existing `audit_mempalace()` `pushback`/`lesson` adoption-count probes as **canonical contract** (no code changes; the probes existed pre-S-0085 between S-0065 and S-0077 but were not documented as required).
- Adversarial prompt-questions in all four posture sections of [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) ŌĆö Fit ("what machinery is silently ignoredŌĆ”"), Gaps ("if a new collaborator joined the project tomorrowŌĆ”"), Infrastructure-without-function ("argue this candidate's retirement"), Bloat ("if the project's machinery were forced to halve in sizeŌĆ”"). Each posture also gains an "Argue retirement / replacement" sub-prompt. Disposition options for Infrastructure-without-function shift from `[retire / convert / preserve]` to `[recommend retire / recommend convert / recommend preserve-with-affirmative-case]` per the user-buffered execution principle.
- "Accumulated pushbacks and lessons" section in [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) with concrete `mempalace_search` commands per [Issue #36](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/36). Audit AI reads `pushback`/`lesson` drawer *content* (not just count) since `last_audit_session`, surfaces clusters in prose, distinguishes "posture not exercised" from "capture surface failing silently" by sampling diary entries when zero captures appear.
- [`engine/build_readiness/adversarial_stance_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/adversarial_stance_first_exercise.md) ŌĆö first-exercise readiness note per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md). Mechanism qualifies under criterion #4 (Consequences span 6 surfaces). T1-A through T1-E (drawer-content reading; user-adjudication-blank; freshness-probe content findings; random-pick procedure; Ōēź1 retire-candidate or adversarially-scrutinized "no candidates") pending the next cadence-fired audit (S-0087 by recommended sequencing). T2-A through T2-D and T3-A through T3-C documented for the first-exercise session to consume.

### Added (S-0084 ŌĆö Issue close-out campaign session S-B: HNSW divergence detection + non-destructive restoration)

- [`engine/tools/probe_palace.py`](tools/probe_palace.py) ŌĆö **divergence-detection extension per the [ADR 0045](adr/0045-shared-state-integrity-discipline.md) S-0084 amendment for [Issue #31](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/31).** The probe now shells out to upstream's `mempalace repair-status` subcommand (read-only by upstream contract; never opens a chromadb client) after the existing chromadb-openability check. Emits `[probe-palace] divergence: HNSW=N1 SQLite=N2 (P%)` on stderr when the upstream tool is available and parseable. Exit code promotes from 0 (healthy) to 1 (suspect) at Ōēź10% divergence; existing 2 (hard-broken) and 139 (segfault) paths unchanged. The `mempalace` binary being absent from PATH is a graceful skip ŌĆö the divergence check returns None and the existing exit-code logic continues. Discovered during planning that the upstream tool already exists; building a probe from scratch was unnecessary reinvention.
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) ŌĆö **new soft-warn category `mempalace_hnsw_divergence`** in `validate_shared_state_health()`. Parses the divergence stderr line emitted by probe_palace.py and emits the soft-warn at Ōēź10% divergence with a body that names the percentage and the BM25-fallback consequence. At Ōēź30% divergence, the body adds the destructive-repair carve-out warning verbatim, naming the S-0078 forensic (99.7% loss observed) and pointing at the supported restoration path. Validator check count rises from 16 to 17.
- [`engine/tools/mempalace_rebuild_hnsw.py`](tools/mempalace_rebuild_hnsw.py) ŌĆö **new tool: non-destructive HNSW rebuild that bypasses `mempalace repair --mode legacy`.** Reads `(embedding_id, document, metadata)` tuples directly from `chroma.sqlite3` via the METADATA-segment join (bypassing the chromadb get-with-embeddings path that fails on divergent palaces with `InternalError: Error finding id`). Deletes the collection preserving its metadata, recreates, and re-adds via `collection.add(ids, documents, metadatas)` WITHOUT explicit embeddings ŌĆö chromadb re-computes via the registered embedding function and writes BOTH SQLite and HNSW segments fresh. Trade-off accepted: rebuilt vectors are not byte-identical to originals (the embedding function may have shifted across versions) ŌĆö but the alternative is to permanently lose the divergent drawers' data, since their original vectors aren't present in the palace. CLI surface: `--palace <required>`, `--collection <repeatable>`, `--batch-size`, `--dry-run`, `--verify-only`, `--embedding-providers`. The `--embedding-providers` flag enables CoreML acceleration on Apple Silicon (50├Ś speedup observed at S-0084 vs CPU-only); the providers override is process-local and doesn't pollute the persisted collection metadata. 5-tier exit-code semantics: 0 success / 1 extraction-short refusal / 2 mid-flight failure (collection deleted, re-add incomplete; restore from snapshot) / 3 post-verify divergence Ōēź1% / 4 non-default embedding function refusal / 5 generic pre-destructive error. 3 unit tests against synthetic chromadb fixtures.
- "Maintenance probes" section in [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) documenting the divergence probe and the destructive-repair carve-out for audit-time consumers.
- "Known issues" entry in [`engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`](operations/mempalace-operations.md) documenting the destructive-repair pattern, forensic detail, restoration path via the new tool, and atomic-rename swap procedure.
- New `mempalace_hnsw_divergence` category in [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md).
- 4 new pytest cases in [`engine/tools/test_probe_palace.py`](tools/test_probe_palace.py) covering: divergence-line emission with stub mempalace binary, exit-code promotion at Ōēź10%, graceful handling when mempalace is absent from PATH, negative-test that probe never invokes bare `mempalace repair`.
- New test file [`engine/tools/test_mempalace_rebuild_hnsw.py`](tools/test_mempalace_rebuild_hnsw.py) with 3 cases: round-trip count + metadata preservation, `--dry-run` writes nothing, refusal on non-default embedding function (per upstream Issue #1255).
- Upstream MemPalace bug filed: [MemPalace/mempalace#1394](https://github.com/MemPalace/mempalace/issues/1394) ŌĆö destructive `mempalace repair --mode legacy` against the version installed at S-0078 wiped 99.7% of SQLite embedding rows; distinct from #1208's 10K cap pattern. Cross-references upstream Issues #1238, #1255, #1263, #1308, #1362, #1092 as adjacent.

### Changed (S-0083 ŌĆö Issue close-out campaign session S-A: cleanup batch + ideation.md retire + tiktoken retire)
- [`engine/tools/scan_mempalace_activity.py`](tools/scan_mempalace_activity.py) ŌĆö **bug fix per [Issue #37](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/37).** Now truncates `current_mempalace.jsonl` after writing the per-session rollup so subsequent sessions don't inherit prior-session calls. Pre-S-0083 the JSONL accumulated indefinitely ŌĆö S-0082's `mempalace_activity.total_calls=7` reflected S-0081's 4 calls plus S-0082's 3. ### Removed (S-0083 ŌĆö `transcript_token_pct` telemetry retired per Issues #21 + #32)
- [`engine/tools/scan_context_telemetry.py`](tools/scan_context_telemetry.py) ŌĆö **deleted** along with its 14 pytest cases at `engine/tools/test_scan_context_telemetry.py`. Empirical justification per Issue #32: the Session-load trend section consumed this telemetry across S-0052 / S-0065 / S-0077 audits and produced **zero behavioral signal** (S-0052 absorbed by triage of >1.0 fluke; S-0065 had 62% None capture rate filed as Issue #21; S-0077 produced "low and stable; no bundling-recommendation change"). The capture itself fluctuated non-deterministically across routine-mode sessions (Issue #21 reframed at S-0077). The defensive surface area required to keep the metric from being misread as live in-session pressure (Issue #11 inline-fix; CLAUDE.md "Posture vs machinery" bullets; the at-read-site cumulative-vs-live framing) outweighed the metric's contribution to actionable decisions.
- `tiktoken>=0.7.0` pin from [`engine/tools/requirements.txt`](tools/requirements.txt). chromadb and mempalace pins remain.
- Step 7b "Capture context telemetry" from [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) and the corresponding step in [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md). Step 8 (outcome_summary fill) now follows step 7a (scope-delivery audit) directly.
- "Session-load trend" section from [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) (both subsections). The cross-session "running too long / too short / high variance" analysis was the consumer that produced no behavioral signal.
- Two `transcript_token_pct` bullets from [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) "Posture vs machinery" ŌĆö the cumulative-vs-live distinction (Issue #11 closure) and the prior-archive-backstop rejection. The mid-session-context-pressure-monitoring bullet is preserved (the underlying gap remains; the operating policy of manual user monitoring is unchanged) but trimmed to remove tiktoken-specific framing.
- `Bash(python3 engine/tools/scan_context_telemetry.py:*)` from [`.claude/settings.json`](../.claude/settings.json) permissions allowlist.

### Removed (S-0083 ŌĆö `product/docs/ideation.md` retired per Issue #29)
- `product/docs/ideation.md` ŌĆö **deleted.** The file was empty (header rows only, no data rows) across S-0001 through S-0077. Its function (capture proposed work / ideas / aspirations) had structurally migrated to GitHub Issues with the `enhancement` label per [ADR 0048](adr/0048-handoff-narrowing-and-github-issues-for-cross-session-deferrals.md) (S-0042). Three consecutive audits (S-0052 / S-0065 / S-0077) preserved the file by reading the empty state as "correct shape" without testing whether the function had migrated ŌĆö a load-bearing instance of the stats-as-proxy-for-function anti-pattern (Issue [#28](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/28)). The S-0077 user feedback flagged the audit failure pattern; the user's S-0083 directive chose full retirement (option A in the issue body) over pointer-ify (option B).
- Inbound-reference cleanup spans 10 active sites: [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) exploration-mode allowlist; [`engine/tools/scan_orphans.py`](tools/scan_orphans.py) `_REGISTER_FILE_NAMES`; [`engine/tools/health_check.py`](tools/health_check.py) `IDEATION_PATH` constant + the unconsumed-ideation-entries audit block (`audit_dead_weight()`); [`engine/tools/test_scan_orphans.py`](tools/test_scan_orphans.py) register-emptiness tests rewritten against `tensions.md`; [`engine/tools/test_health_check.py`](tools/test_health_check.py) ideation tests dropped + `synthetic_repo` fixture monkeypatch removed; [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) `register-empty` axis description; [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) capture-flow guidance redirected to GitHub Issues; [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) mirror; [`README.md`](../README.md) project-structure diagram + pre-commit-hook description. Historical refs in [`HANDOFF.md`](../HANDOFF.md), [`engine/ENGINE_LOG.md`](ENGINE_LOG.md), archived `docs/health-checks/*`, and the S-0042 build_readiness retrospective are preserved unchanged per their respective lifecycles.

### Added (S-0082 ŌĆö Phase 5 production audit master plan; T-PHASE-5-AUDIT routine target lands)
- [`engine/build_readiness/phase_5_production_audit.md`](build_readiness/phase_5_production_audit.md) ŌĆö master-plan gate report for the Phase 5 graph production audit per S-0081 gate's PROCEED recommendation. Contents: scope/anti-scope, fixed SEP-anchored prompt template (per-edge + per-node, copy-paste-discipline rather than paraphrase to prevent AI-generic critique), fixed evidence file schema, sample-size policy table (35% per-subdomain density per S-0081 expansion rule given 47% cross-bridge defect rate; ~265 edges + ~96 nodes + 10 hubs reviewed across the 12 sessions), three diagnostic syllabus targets (Gettier counterexamples to JTB / modal realism / social_contract_theory ŌĆö `social_contract_theory` substituted for absent `free_speech` per S-0081 coverage finding), Tier 1/2/3 triage (T1-A through T1-F resolved; T2-A through T2-E codified; T3-A through T3-F deferred to closeout), 4 pre-listed audit-system-input proposals (`edge_evidence_empty`, `discipline_label_node_at_root`, `prereq_direction_summary_inconsistency` (NLP-flagged, possibly defer), `historical_node_as_prereq_source`), structural-reopen pre-flag for `historical_influence` predicate activation (S-0081 extrapolation: ~19 of 71 cross-bridges historical-not-pedagogical exceeds the Ōēź10 ADR-warranting threshold), forward pointers to closeout (final reports, Issue filing, ADR memos, README multi-class restructure per Issue #26).

Per-task scope_lock pinned to single evidence file under `engine/build_readiness/phase_5_production_audit_evidence/<task>.md`; criteria are `file_exists` + `validate_passes`. Closeout (interactive) is NOT a target task ŌĆö T1-F discipline. check_target.py parses cleanly: 12 tasks pending, validate_passes already true, file_exists pending evidence-session work.

### Added (S-0081 ŌĆö Phase 5 production audit warrant gate; novel report class introduced)
- [`engine/build_readiness/phase_5_production_audit_gate.md`](build_readiness/phase_5_production_audit_gate.md) ŌĆö gate report for the proposed 14-session Phase 5 graph production audit. Single-session preflight per the user-approved plan at `~/.claude/plans/exploration-session-phase-5-flickering-newell.md`: 15-edge cross-bridge sample (md5-deterministic) + 5-edge within-domain epistemology sample with SEP-anchored review + topology pass (per-subdomain degree distribution, top-10 hubs, three syllabus traces). Threshold-rule outcome: **PROCEED** ŌĆö 8 substantive findings of 20 sampled edges (40%); 4 of 15 cross-bridges historical-not-pedagogical (extrapolating to ~19 of 71, exceeding the Ōēź10 ADR-warranting threshold for `cross_domain_dependency` structural reopen); one clean reversed edge (`propositional_attitude ŌåÆ proposition` contradicts node summaries); 0/536 edges with evidence-field text (graph-wide discipline gap; gate-feasible audit-system-input proposal); free speech absent from political philosophy (coverage defect); discipline-label nodes acting as syllabus-trace roots (granularity-mismatch defect class). Within-domain epistemology: 0 findings of 5 sampled ŌĆö defects concentrate in cross-bridges. Forward inputs to the master-plan session pre-listed: per-subdomain density 35% (cross-bridge defect rate 47% triggers plan's expansion rule); diagnostic-target swap for absent free_speech; 4 audit-system-input soft-warn proposals pre-listed; structural reopen pre-flagged (likely `historical_influence` predicate activation rather than `cross_domain_dependency` introduction).
- Audit-warrant gate is a novel build-readiness report class ŌĆö sibling to standard build-readiness gates (per [ADR 0040](adr/0040-build-readiness-gate-before-substantive-build-sessions.md)) and closeout reports (e.g., [`phase_5_closeout.md`](build_readiness/phase_5_closeout.md)). Structurally parallels Tier 1/2/3 triage adapted to PROCEED/RESCOPE/CANCEL outcomes; consumer is a future gate session (the audit master-plan), not a build session. The pattern is reusable for any future production-audit consideration (Phase 6 / 7+ outputs).
- MemPalace decision drawer filed at `paideia/decisions/drawer_paideia_decisions_f3a357a5efea52e783db689a` recording the PROCEED outcome, the predeclared threshold rule, and the forward-inputs to the master-plan session. Diary entry topic `S-0081-audit-warrant-gate` filed in agent `claude` wing `paideia`.

### Removed (S-0080 ŌĆö cleanup of misleading S-0079 artifacts)
- Deleted `engine/tools/recover_mempalace_from_transcript.py` and `engine/tools/test_recover_mempalace_from_transcript.py`. The wrapper's `--prompt` mode (analytical-voice template) and path-resolution logic encoded the wrong recovery shape: a separate session reads transcripts and writes drawers about another session. The user's actual ask was a brief reflection prompt to paste into ORIGINAL sessions still accessible to the user ŌĆö original session writes its own MemPalace entries in its own voice (no separate session, no transcript re-reading, honest first-person attributed to its own `S-NNNN`). With the dispatch shape removed, neither the prompt template nor the path-resolution logic is useful.
- Deleted `engine/docs/audits/mempalace-recovery-guide-user-driven.md`. Encoded the same wrong shape as the wrapper. Replaced by a corrective section in [`engine/docs/audits/mempalace-attribution-S0001-to-S0077.md`](docs/audits/mempalace-attribution-S0001-to-S0077.md) explaining the actual recovery shape; the brief reflection prompt itself lives in the chat history where it was developed (the user pastes it directly into each missing session).

### Added (S-0078 ŌĆö MemPalace mechanical adoption checks land; closes Issues #27 and #20)
- [ADR 0056](adr/0056-mempalace-mechanical-adoption-checks.md) ŌĆö engine ADR for MemPalace mechanical adoption checks across all session types (interactive `/start-engine` + routine `/start-routine`). End-to-end mechanization via four layers: (1) `PostToolUse` hook on `mcp__mempalace__.*` writes per-session JSONL telemetry; (2) rollup tool writes `mempalace_activity` archive field at shutdown step 0; (3) `validate.py --final-check` (gated CLI flag) emits two soft-warns and one hard-fail; (4) `audit_archive_structured_fields.py` parameterized to declarative `REQUIRED_ARCHIVE_FIELDS` list. Closes [Issue #27](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/27) (12/16 Phase 5 routine sessions silently skipped diary write per S-0077 audit confirmation) and [Issue #20](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/20) (parameterize archive-history audit). User-adjudicated forks at plan time: mixed enforcement (soft-warn for boot query / diary read; hard-fail for diary write with acknowledgement-token escape hatch); rename `diary_skipped` ŌåÆ `mempalace_diary_write_skipped` with one-shot backfill across 32 archives; recovery scope ALL ~45 flagged-as-missing sessions; recovery method transcript-crawl via Claude subagents.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/post-mempalace-tool-use.sh`](tools/hooks/post-mempalace-tool-use.sh) ŌĆö new PostToolUse hook script. Reads payload from stdin, extracts `tool_name`, appends one JSONL line per `mcp__mempalace__*` call to `engine/session/current_mempalace.jsonl`. Always exits 0; never blocks. Same architectural pattern as `post-adr-write.sh` and `post-state-edit.sh` per [ADR 0043](adr/0043-hook-architecture.md). Wired in `.claude/settings.json` PostToolUse with matcher `mcp__mempalace__.*`.
- [`engine/tools/scan_mempalace_activity.py`](tools/scan_mempalace_activity.py) ŌĆö new shutdown-step-0 rollup tool. Reads `current_mempalace.jsonl`, counts calls per tool, writes `mempalace_activity` field into `current.json` with shape `{search_calls, diary_read_calls, diary_write_calls, add_drawer_calls, status_calls, list_drawers_calls, other_calls, total_calls, first_call_ts, last_call_ts}`. Symmetric to `scan_context_telemetry.py` per ADR 0049. 13 pytests.
- [`engine/tools/migrate_diary_skipped_archive_field.py`](tools/migrate_diary_skipped_archive_field.py) ŌĆö one-shot rename migration: renames `diary_skipped` ŌåÆ `mempalace_diary_write_skipped` in `outcome_summary_soft_warns` across every existing archive. Surgical text-based key removal preserves formatting and UTF-8 (json.dumps would re-escape Unicode and normalize compact-vs-indented arrays); handles last-key edge case (strips prior trailing comma when removing the last dict entry). 10 pytests including unicode-preservation and last-key-strip. Migration ran cleanly against 32 archives.
- [`engine/build_readiness/mempalace_mechanical_adoption_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/mempalace_mechanical_adoption_first_exercise.md) ŌĆö first-exercise readiness note per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md) (qualifies on trigger criteria #2, #3, and #4: introduces new validator categories with session-side discipline; introduces new state file the boot procedure reads; Consequences span 16 surfaces). T1-A (interactive first-exercise) closes at S-0078 shutdown ŌĆö `validate.py --final-check` passes cleanly with `total_calls=6 search=1 diary_read=1 diary_write=1 add_drawer=3` after the hook fires for this session's MemPalace MCP calls. T1-B (routine first-exercise) closes at next routine fire post-S-0078.
- New `engine/tools/test_validate_mempalace_adoption.py` (9 pytests), `engine/tools/test_scan_mempalace_activity.py` (13), `engine/tools/test_migrate_diary_skipped_archive_field.py` (10), and 19 new tests in `engine/tools/test_audit_archive_structured_fields.py` (parameterized field set + archive-history mode + per-field absence). 62 new tests; 757 total pass.

### Added (S-0077 ŌĆö 5th formal project health-check audit; cadence cleared; first content in `tools-validate-interpretation.md` Persistent-warn annotation section)
- [`docs/health-checks/S-0077.md`](../docs/health-checks/S-0077.md) ŌĆö 5th formal project health-check audit (after S-0030 / S-0041 / S-0052 / S-0065). Audit window S-0066 ŌåÆ S-0076 (11 sessions; first audit dominated by a sustained routine-only run end-to-end). Surfaced four non-obvious findings: **(A)** STATE.md narrative-surface ADR count drift ŌĆö line 11 said "54/19/35," line 75 said "52/17/35," reality 56/21/35 (validator's `adr_index_consistency` audits READMEs but not STATE.md prose); **fixed inline**; meta-pattern named (a narrative claim the validator can't audit will drift even when written by sessions that know better). **(B)** `mode` field absent on S-0069 archive (and S-0065) ŌĆö extends prior audit's structured-field-consistency Finding A pattern to a different field; ADR 0051 added `mode` without extending `audit_archive_structured_fields.py`; strengthens cost-benefit for Issue [#20](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/20) closure. ### Added (S-0072 ŌĆö routine close-out apparatus: parent main FF post-push and post-close worktree sweep)
- [`engine/tools/routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/routine_lifecycle_push.py) ŌĆö added `parent_ff()` helper and post-push invocation in `main()` for all three modes (eager-claim, deliverable, close). Closes the asymmetry vs interactive close where parent's local main was being left stale because the routine wrapper pushes from inside a linked worktree on a feature branch (`HEAD:main`). Best-effort: parent FF failure (parent on a non-target branch, uncommitted-change conflicts) is logged but does NOT propagate to the wrapper exit code; boot-freshness remains the safety net per [ADR 0052](adr/0052-routine-boot-freshness-and-concurrency-defense.md). After this change, parent main acquires `merge claude/<branch>: Fast-forward` entries (matching the interactive shape) instead of `merge refs/remotes/origin/main: Fast-forward` (the next session's reactive boot-freshness recovery). Symptom diagnosed in this conversation's own boot-freshness FF surface: every routine fire was needing the FF to catch up.
- [`engine/tools/routine_worktree_sweep.py`](tools/routine_worktree_sweep.py) ŌĆö new tool, called from inside the worktree as the last action of routine close (after the close push and lock release). Removes the current session's worktree and its `claude/<name>` branch with the same pre-flight checks as `sweep_worktrees.sh` (claude/* branch, working tree clean, branch merged into main); refusals exit 2 with explicit reasons, generic git errors exit 5, both logged-and-continue (close has already succeeded ŌĆö sweep is best-effort). The tool chdirs to parent BEFORE calling `git worktree remove` so child-process forks from this Python process don't fail on macOS once the worktree's CWD is unlinked. Closes the auto-clean follow-on named in [Issue #16](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/16).
- [`engine/tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py) ŌĆö 7 new pytests for parent FF (32 total). Coverage: parent-path resolution from worktree vs parent, parent_ff success advances main, no-op when called from parent, refusal when parent on non-main branch, end-to-end main() with parent_ff success and failure paths.
- [`engine/tools/test_routine_worktree_sweep.py`](tools/test_routine_worktree_sweep.py) ŌĆö new test file, 18 pytests. Covers helper unit behavior, all preflight refusal paths (parent invocation, dirty tree, non-claude/* branch, unmerged branch, detached HEAD), main() success / dry-run / refusal / cwd-default, and the chdir-before-sweep contract.

### Changed (S-0069 ŌĆö STATE.md size maintenance; rolling-window trim policy)
- [`engine/STATE.md`](STATE.md) ŌĆö **one-time trim from ~35,456 tokens to ~6,000 tokens (25,155 bytes / 106 lines).** Four targeted edits: (1) 'Current phase' cell collapsed from 3,500-word session-history blob to a current-state summary sentence + ENGINE_LOG.md pointer; (2) all 13 'Prior build session' and 'Prior-prior build session' rows removed (S-0043 ŌåÆ S-0067; exact duplicates of ENGINE_LOG.md entries ŌĆö the rolling-window design had no drop policy, so rows accumulated without bound); (3) stale historical paragraph from 'Next session work item' section pruned (referenced P5-06 as blocked, S-0059 context, and apply-mechanics findings all superseded by S-0064/S-0066/S-0068); (4) 'After S-0045' mini-changelog subsection removed (all entries fully captured in ENGINE_LOG.md). Nothing is lost: trimmed content is preserved in ENGINE_LOG.md narratives and `engine/session/archive/S-*.json` machine-readable records. Root cause: two accumulation patterns with no drop bound; MCP tool read limit (~25,000 tokens) exceeded at S-0069 boot. Deliverable commit `b28d9ea`.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) ŌĆö **rolling-window trim policy added** to the "Update STATE.md" step (step 4). Policy: after each session close, drop every row labeled 'Prior build session' or 'Prior-prior build session' ŌĆö keep only the new 'Last build session' row plus one 'Prior build session' row at most. If STATE.md still exceeds ~20,000 tokens after the row drop, also collapse the 'Current phase' cell to the current-state summary form. Prevents the accumulation pattern that caused the S-0069 overflow from recurring.

### Added (S-0064 ŌĆö apply-migration wrapper unblocks Phase 5 routine-mode after Production Reads gate regression)
- [`engine/adr/0055-apply-migration-wrapping-against-production-reads-gate.md`](adr/0055-apply-migration-wrapping-against-production-reads-gate.md) ŌĆö **new ADR.** Names the auto-mode classifier's "Production Reads" gate as the failure mode (denies MCP supabase tools + ad-hoc psycopg from routine context with "Production Reads requires explicit user approval"; the gate is undocumented but real per a built-in `soft_deny` default; not configurable via per-MCP-tool allow rules). Introduces `engine/tools/apply_migration.py` as a parallel layer to ADR 0054's `routine_lifecycle_push.py`: harness gates Bash command surface, not subprocess-spawned operations from inside a permitted python tool. Trigger criterion #4 satisfied (8 surfaces).
- [`engine/tools/apply_migration.py`](tools/apply_migration.py) ŌĆö the wrapper itself, ~360 lines. Three modes (default apply / `--dry-run` / `--force`). Mechanically shape-verifies HEAD before applying. Failure-mode discrimination via exit codes 0/2/3/4/5/6/7. Closes [Issue #18](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/18).
- [`engine/tools/test_apply_migration.py`](tools/test_apply_migration.py) ŌĆö 24 pytests against psycopg-stub fixtures; stub `__spec__` set via `importlib.machinery.ModuleSpec` to bypass transitive `find_spec` from `_venv_reexec.ensure_venv_python`; module-level `_StubError` classes for shared exception identity.
- [`engine/build_readiness/apply_migration_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/apply_migration_first_exercise.md) ŌĆö mechanism-first-exercise gate report per ADR 0053. T1-B/C/D/E resolved at S-0064; T1-A pending first routine fire post-S-0064.

Per Issue #16 plan and ADR 0054 readiness note, the probe commit is the forensic record of the empirical bypass test; deletion holds until the bypass is verified working in routine context.
- **Net change**: 28 ŌåÆ 3 `claude/*` branches; 22 ŌåÆ 3 worktrees (current S-0062 + 2 dirty pending user adjudication).

### Added (S-0060 ŌĆö routine lifecycle-push wrapper; closes harness Default Branch Push gate)
- [`engine/adr/0054-lifecycle-push-wrapping-against-default-branch-push-gate.md`](adr/0054-lifecycle-push-wrapping-against-default-branch-push-gate.md) ŌĆö **new ADR.** Names the local-routine "Default Branch Push" gate as the failure mode that blocked S-0059's eager-claim push from a routine session. Introduces `routine_lifecycle_push.py` as a fourth mechanical layer in [ADR 0052](adr/0052-routine-boot-freshness-and-concurrency-defense.md)'s freshness/lock/recovery family. The wrapper performs the push via `subprocess.run(["git", "push", ...])` from inside a permitted python tool ŌĆö the harness gate inspects Bash command surface, not subprocess-spawned git operations. Each of three modes (`eager-claim`, `deliverable`, `close`) mechanically shape-verifies HEAD before pushing; refuses with explicit reject reason and exit 2 on any verification failure ŌĆö actively safer than raw `git push` for lifecycle commits. Failure-mode discrimination via exit codes 0/2/3/4/5: 0 success, 2 verification refused (HANDOFF; no retry), 3 push rejected by remote (gate fired despite hypothesis OR non-fast-forward race), 4 network failure (retry once after 5s), 5 generic git error. Trigger-criterion evaluation per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md) section: qualifies under #4 (Consequences span Ōēź 5 tooling files) ŌĆö first-exercise gate report is mandatory before unattended use.
- [`engine/tools/routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/routine_lifecycle_push.py) ŌĆö **the wrapper itself, ~410 lines.** Three modes per ADR 0054. Each verifier runs `git log`, `git rev-list --count`, `git status --porcelain`, `git diff --name-status` against `origin/main`, and (for eager-claim and close) reads register_state.json before and after via `git show`. The deliverable mode imports `check_routine_scope` for path-matching parity with the boot-time scope check. On verification refusal: prints `[routine-lifecycle-push] REFUSED ({mode}): <reason>` to stderr, names the local commit SHA, and exits 2 ŌĆö does NOT amend, reset, or otherwise modify the repo (matches `routine_eager_claim_recovery.py`'s posture: bounded shape only; outside the shape, refuse).
- [`engine/tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py`](tools/test_routine_lifecycle_push.py) ŌĆö **21 pytests against tmp-dir bare-repo + clone fixtures.** Per the user's S-0060 directive ("test, test, test"). Coverage: 3 well-formed accepts (one per mode); 12 shape-verification rejects covering distinct predicates per mode (eager-claim: two-commits-ahead, subject-pattern-wrong, diff-touches-outside-set, register-state-doesnt-bump-one, current-json-already-existed; deliverable: chore(session)-prefix-reserved, subject-not-conventional-commits, path-outside-scope_lock, working-tree-dirty; close: archive-not-created, current-json-not-deleted, register-state-doesnt-flip, diff-touches-arbitrary); 3 push-failure paths (non-fast-forward returns 3, unreachable remote returns 4, missing remote returns 5); 3 edge cases (main refuses with exit 2 without pushing; --dry-run verifies but does not push). All green. Fixture pattern matches `test_routine_eager_claim_recovery.py`.
- [`engine/tools/probe_push_gate.py`](tools/probe_push_gate.py) ŌĆö **Phase 0 empirical probe (~40 lines + 8 pytests).** Three modes: --dry-run (default, safe anywhere), --actually-push (empty commit + push to throwaway branch `claude/probe-push-gate-<UTC-timestamp>`), --actually-push --target-main (load-bearing test: pushes empty commit to main via subprocess). Phase 0 Run 2 result (S-0060): subprocess push to throwaway branch succeeded from interactive context (commit `dafaad6` on remote ref `claude/probe-push-gate-20260505T045706Z`); local HEAD soft-reset back to eager-claim. Phase 0 Run 3 (load-bearing ŌĆö subprocess push to main from routine context) deferred to first routine fire post-S-0060 per the readiness note.
- [`engine/tools/test_probe_push_gate.py`](tools/test_probe_push_gate.py) ŌĆö 8 pytests covering probe modes against tmp-dir bare-repo fixtures. All green.
- [`engine/build_readiness/routine_lifecycle_push_first_exercise.md`](build_readiness/routine_lifecycle_push_first_exercise.md) ŌĆö **mechanism-first-exercise gate report per [ADR 0053](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md).** Covers the wrapper's pre-flight: trigger-criterion evaluation (qualifies under #4), Phase 0 empirical findings (Run 1 baseline, Run 2 interactive subprocess success, Run 3 deferred-with-rationale), Tier 1 / Tier 2 / Tier 3 triage, cold-review prompts. T1-A (subprocess-bypass verification for routine context) closes at Phase 2 wrapper verification.

- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0020_seed_ethics_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0020_seed_ethics_part1.sql) ŌĆö **sixth Phase 5 seed migration; first ethics file.** 28 nodes + 34 edges across two layers per [phase_5.md](build_readiness/phase_5.md) T1-B. Foundation (1): morality (subdomain umbrella). Metaethics (12): metaethics, moral_realism, moral_anti_realism, error_theory (Mackie 1977 ŌĆö argument from queerness + relativity), expressivism (Ayer 1936 / Stevenson 1944 / Hare 1952 / Blackburn quasi-realism / Gibbard plan-expressivism; Frege-Geach problem central technical challenge), moral_naturalism (Cornell ŌĆö Boyd 1988 / Brink 1989 / Sturgeon 1985), moral_non_naturalism (Moore 1903 PRINCIPIA ETHICA / Parfit 2011 ON WHAT MATTERS), open_question_argument (Frankena 1939 "naturalistic fallacy"), moral_epistemology (intuitionism / coherentism / reliabilism / skepticism ŌĆö the four approaches), motivational_internalism (Hare 1952 / Blackburn 1984 / Smith 1994), motivational_externalism (Brink 1989 / Svavarsd├│ttir 1999), is_ought_distinction (Hume 1739 TREATISE; Searle 1964 promising-counterexample debate). Normative theory (15): normative_ethics, consequentialism (Williams 1973 integrity objection), utilitarianism (Bentham 1789 / Mill 1861; act-vs-rule; trolley / experience-machine / demandingness), hedonism (Nozick 1974 experience machine; Mill higher-vs-lower pleasures; bridge to philosophy-of-mind on consciousness and to economics on welfare), deontology (Ross 1930 prima facie duties refinement; agent-centered restrictions/options), kantian_ethics (Kant 1785 GROUNDWORK / 1788 CRITIQUE OF PRACTICAL REASON; pure practical reason; rigorism), categorical_imperative (Universal Law / Humanity-as-End / Kingdom of Ends; Korsgaard 1996 unification), virtue_ethics (Anscombe 1958 / Foot / MacIntyre 1981 / Hursthouse 1999 revival; situationism critique), eudaimonia (Aristotle's NICOMACHEAN ETHICS; ergon argument; objective achievement not subjective satisfaction), practical_wisdom (Aristotelian phronesis; perception / deliberation / desire-integration; McDowell 1979 / Nussbaum 1990 contemporary defenses), contractualism (Scanlon 1998 WHAT WE OWE TO EACH OTHER; aggregation problem; distinguished from political social contract tradition), divine_command_theory (Christian Adams 1999 / Islamic Asharite / Jewish; Euthyphro dilemma; modified DCT separating good-from-nature from obligations-from-commands), ethical_egoism (Hobbes / Rand / Brink 1989; Parfit 1984 self-defeating charge), moral_particularism (Dancy 1993 MORAL REASONS / 2004 ETHICS WITHOUT PRINCIPLES; holism about moral reasons), supererogation (the structural concept testing whether normative theories accommodate "above and beyond"; demandingness objection to consequentialism; Wolf 1982 / Heyd 1982 / Archer 2018). All 28 nodes `confidence_level=INTERPRETED` (mirrors P5-01a/P5-01b/P5-02a/P5-02b/P5-03's distribution at 100%; phase_5.md T2-B floor satisfied); all 34 edges `pedagogical_prerequisite`. `domain[]` exactly `{ethics}` for every node ŌĆö cross-domain bridges to deontic_logic / free_will / moral_responsibility / knowledge / belief / justification / political philosophy deferred to P5-11. `provenance='ai-seed'` everywhere. `graph_version` 6 ŌåÆ 7 in same transaction as the 62 INSERTs. Edge structure: 5-tier layered DAG (T0 morality; T1 metaethics + normative_ethics; T2 nine substructure ŌĆö moral_realism / moral_anti_realism / is_ought_distinction / consequentialism / deontology / virtue_ethics / contractualism / ethical_egoism / divine_command_theory / moral_particularism ŌĆö wait, ten, with supererogation at T3 because deontology and consequentialism feed it; recount: T2 has nine because moral_particularism gets reach from both normative_ethics and virtue_ethics so it's T3, and supererogation gets reach from deontology and consequentialism so it's T3); T3 nine ŌĆö moral_epistemology / moral_naturalism / moral_non_naturalism / error_theory / utilitarianism / kantian_ethics / eudaimonia / practical_wisdom / moral_particularism / supererogation; T4 four ŌĆö open_question_argument / motivational_internalism / hedonism / categorical_imperative; T5 two ŌĆö motivational_externalism / expressivism. Every edge points from a lower tier to a higher tier so the Kosaraju SCC check confirms acyclicity post-apply. Authored under task P5-04a of `T-PHASE-5` per [`engine/build_readiness/phase_5.md`](build_readiness/phase_5.md). Apply mechanics: ~70KB body too large for single MCP `apply_migration`; applied via four `execute_sql` calls (UPDATE settings; INSERT 13 nodes; INSERT 15 nodes; INSERT 34 edges) in FK-safe order, then `apply_migration` with name `0020_seed_ethics_part1` and no-op body (`SELECT 1;` plus contract-block comment) recorded the migration name in `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations`. SQL escape bug caught and fixed pre-apply: `is_ought_distinction.teaching_notes` initially had `Mackie's queerness` (single apostrophe) inside a single-quoted string literal; caught by `awk '/^--/ {next} 1' | grep "[a-zA-Z]'[a-zA-Z]"` sweep across non-comment lines; fixed to `Mackie''s` before any apply call. Live verification post-apply: 160 total nodes, 206 total edges in `paideia-dev`.
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/ROUTING.md`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/ROUTING.md) ŌĆö **per-session narrative entry for S-0058.** Documents the two-layer (metaethics + normative theory) decomposition with canonical anchors per cluster, the 5-tier layered DAG edge structure (2 foundation + 4 metaethics-substructure + 11 within-metaethics + 7 normative-umbrellas + 2 within-consequentialism + 2 within-deontology + 3 within-virtue + 3 supererogation = 34), the cross-domain deferrals to P5-11 (deontologyŌåödeontic_logic, kantian_ethicsŌåöphilosophy-of-mind on practical reason, virtue_ethicsŌåöpolitical-philosophy on social conditions for flourishing, contractualismŌåöpolitical-philosophy on social contract tradition, moral_realismŌåömetaphysics on moral properties, moral_naturalismŌåöphilosophy-of-science on empirical moral inquiry, moral_epistemologyŌåöepistemology on knowledge-belief-justification, free_willŌåömoral_responsibility from P5-02b presupposed by every normative theory's account of moral agency), the `confidence_level` distribution (100% INTERPRETED), the `graph_version` increment 6ŌåÆ7 with live totals 160/206, the chunked-apply mechanics with the apply_migration marker pattern, the SQL escape bug catch, and the two-commit pattern continued from S-0053/S-0054/S-0056/S-0057.

### Added (S-0055 ŌĆö routine-mode hardening; Issues #12, #13, #14, #15 closed)
- [`engine/adr/0052-routine-boot-freshness-and-concurrency-defense.md`](adr/0052-routine-boot-freshness-and-concurrency-defense.md) ŌĆö **Three-layer routine-boot hardening**, per Issue #15. Diagnosis correction landed mid-session: the original "concurrent eager-claim race" framing was wrong ŌĆö the prior session had already closed before the loser started. Actual failure was boot-time staleness. Layers: (1) `routine_boot_freshness.py` mechanical fast-forward (primary; addresses actual S-0054 failure mode); (2) `routine_lock.py` O_EXCL atomic lockfile with stale-after-1h auto-eviction (defense-in-depth per user direction); (3) `routine_eager_claim_recovery.py` mechanically-verified bounded reset on push-rejection (residual). All three hooked into routine-mode-lifecycle Skill steps 0a, 0b, step-8 push-rejection branch, step-11 lock-release.
- [`engine/adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md`](adr/0053-mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md) ŌĆö **Mechanism-first-exercise gate**, per Issue #12 + S-0052 health-check Finding A. Sibling to ADR 0040's build-readiness gate; mechanism-triggered (vs phase-triggered). Resolves all four open sub-questions in-band: disjunctive trigger criterion (new session mode / new validator soft-warn category dependent on session-side discipline / new state file boot reads / Consequences spans Ōēź3 ops docs OR Ōēź5 tools); same Tier 1/2/3 triage rubric; deliberation lives in this ADR + new ops doc + per-mechanism reports under `engine/build_readiness/`; gate fires once per qualifying mechanism. Cross-cutting ADRs going forward must include a trigger-criterion evaluation block.
- [`engine/operations/mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md`](operations/mechanism-first-exercise-gate.md) ŌĆö **Layer 1 procedure for ADR 0053.** When the gate fires; how to fire the mechanism interactively against real state; how to observe and instrument; how to triage findings; how to author the gate report at `engine/build_readiness/<mechanism>_first_exercise.md`.
- [`engine/tools/_venv_reexec.py`](tools/_venv_reexec.py) ŌĆö **Auto-reexec helper for psycopg-importing tools**, per Issue #14. `ensure_venv_python(required_module="psycopg")` walks up from the script's directory to find `.venv/bin/python3` (worktree-local first, main-repo fallback ŌĆö same precedence as `scrub_env.sh`) and `os.execv`'s the venv interpreter when the required module isn't importable. Subtle bug fix during smoke testing: pass the symlink path (not resolved path) as argv[0] so Python uses pyvenv.cfg to bootstrap site-packages ŌĆö resolving the symlink loads the underlying interpreter without venv site-packages.
- [`engine/tools/audit_archive_structured_fields.py`](tools/audit_archive_structured_fields.py) ŌĆö **Hard-fail close on missing `outcome_summary_soft_warns`**, per Issue #13. Symmetric in shape to `audit_handoff_dispositions.py`. Pre-commit hook fires on closing commits via `git show :engine/session/archive/S-NNNN.json | python3 ... --from-stdin`. Defends ADR 0042's persistent-warn surface against silent field-absence lapses (S-0043 ŌåÆ S-0047 case study). Optional secondary advisory when field is empty AND session had Ōēź3 commits.
- [`engine/tools/routine_boot_freshness.py`](tools/routine_boot_freshness.py) ŌĆö Layer 1 of ADR 0052 fix. Best-effort `git fetch`, then ancestor check, then `git merge --ff-only origin/main` if behind. Diverged HEAD exits 2 (refuse boot).
- [`engine/tools/routine_lock.py`](tools/routine_lock.py) ŌĆö Layer 2 of ADR 0052 fix. CLI: `acquire | release | check`. Default lockfile at `.claude/routine.lock` (gitignored under `.claude/*`). Stale-after default 1 hour.
- [`engine/tools/routine_eager_claim_recovery.py`](tools/routine_eager_claim_recovery.py) ŌĆö Layer 3 of ADR 0052 fix. Verifies eager-claim-race shape (one commit ahead, both sides claim same slot) before performing bounded `git reset --hard origin/main`. Whitelisted carve-out to routine-mode destructive-action posture per CLAUDE.md.
- 5 new test files (`test__venv_reexec.py`, `test_audit_archive_structured_fields.py`, `test_routine_boot_freshness.py`, `test_routine_lock.py`, `test_routine_eager_claim_recovery.py`) ŌĆö 39 new tests total, all passing.

### Added (S-0054 ŌĆö Phase 5 metaphysics core seed; P5-02a complete)
- [`product/seed-graph/migrations/0030_seed_metaphysics_part1.sql`](../product/seed-graph/migrations/0030_seed_metaphysics_part1.sql) ŌĆö **third Phase 5 seed migration; first metaphysics file.** 27 nodes + 30 edges covering the four core metaphysics pillars per [phase_5.md](build_readiness/phase_5.md) T1-B. Four clusters: (1) being / ontology (metaphysics, ontology, existence, substance, property, relation, event, abstract_object, concrete_object); (2) identity (numerical_identity, leibniz_law, persistence, endurantism, perdurantism, temporal_parts, ship_of_theseus); (3) causation (causation, humean_regularity_theory, counterfactual_theory_of_causation, causal_powers); (4) time (time, a_theory_of_time, b_theory_of_time, presentism, eternalism, growing_block_theory, mctaggarts_paradox). All 27 nodes `confidence_level=INTERPRETED` (mirrors P5-01a/P5-01b distribution at 100%; phase_5.md T2-B floor satisfied); all 30 edges `pedagogical_prerequisite`. `domain[]` exactly `{metaphysics}` for every node ŌĆö cross-domain bridges deferred to P5-11. `provenance='ai-seed'` everywhere. `graph_version` 3 ŌåÆ 4 in same transaction as the 57 INSERTs. - **GitHub Issue #14** (`tech-debt`) ŌĆö **routine-fired check_target.py / validate.py silently fail when venv not on PATH.** Surfaced at S-0054 boot: bare `python3 engine/tools/check_target.py` resolves to system Python (3.9, no psycopg) and emits "psycopg not available; cannot verify" FAIL on every `migration_applied` criterion ŌĆö false-FAIL classification that would mark a successfully-completed task as `blocked` at step-10 verification. Fix is sourcing `engine/tools/scrub_env.sh` before invocation, OR (better) auto-reexec under venv Python at the top of the affected scripts. Outside P5-02a's `scope_lock`; filed for the next interactive `/start-engine` session per ADR 0048 routing. User direction: "file the issue for review later."
