### Added (S-0051 ŌĆö Issue #9 fix unblocks P5-01a; Issue #10 boot-staleness check; label optimization)
- **Boot-time worktree-staleness check** in [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) (Issue #10). Runs `git fetch --no-tags --quiet origin main` then `git merge-base --is-ancestor origin/main HEAD`; emits a LOUD attention block to stderr when HEAD is behind origin/main, surfacing the recovery command (`git fetch && git merge --ff-only origin/main`) inline. Status logged to `.claude/logs/session-start.log` as `stale_check=up-to-date|behind-N|fetch-failed|not-a-git-repo|not-run`. Best-effort (network failure exits silently with log line; never blocks). Closes the gap that surfaced at S-0051 boot: a worktree created before a remote update sees stale shared-state files (`register_state.json`, `current.json`, `auto_target.json`) and the AI proceeds on stale truth. Filed Issue #10 then fixed in same session per S-0051 user direction "no more session cascade for every bug ŌĆö fix it here."
- **Two GitHub Issue label-taxonomy entries with authoring procedures**: `documentation` (doc improvements/bugs/cleanup) and `question` (genuine open questions needing deliberation before action shape clarifies). Both join the existing 6 type labels in [`engine/operations/issue-discipline.md`](operations/issue-discipline.md) "Label taxonomy" table.
- **New "Reactive-only labels" section** in [`engine/operations/issue-discipline.md`](operations/issue-discipline.md) framing `duplicate`, `invalid`, `wontfix` as triage-time-applied (no authoring procedure). Documents the dropping of community labels (`good first issue`, `help wanted`) at S-0051.
- **`count_upstream_bugs` helper + 2 new tests** in [`engine/tools/scan_issue_backlog.py`](tools/scan_issue_backlog.py) + [`engine/tools/test_scan_issue_backlog.py`](tools/test_scan_issue_backlog.py). The helper counts issues tagged BOTH `bug` AND `upstream`; the new format_fyi_line subtracts that from the bug count and surfaces upstream separately. Tests cover the subtraction including floor-at-zero defensive case.
- **Regression test `test_migration_applied_queries_name_column`** in [`engine/tools/test_check_target.py`](tools/test_check_target.py) ŌĆö mocks `psycopg.connect`, asserts SQL passed to `cursor.execute` references the `name` column with the descriptive id; locks Issue #9's fix.

### Added (S-0049 ŌĆö walk-up `.env` loader; Issue #8 closed)
- [`engine/tools/load_env.py`](tools/load_env.py) ŌĆö **new walk-up `.env` loader.** `find_dotenv` walks up from cwd up to a 10-ancestor depth cap looking for the nearest `.env`; `load_dotenv` parses (reusing `parse_env` from S-0048's [`setup_env.py`](tools/setup_env.py) ŌĆö no new dep, no duplicate parser) and applies values to `os.environ` for keys not already set (or all if `override=True`); `load_dotenv_walk_up` combines the two as the standard call site for tool main(). Module also has a `__main__` diagnostic that prints the located `.env` and its populated keys.
- [`engine/tools/test_load_env.py`](tools/test_load_env.py) ŌĆö **14 tests.** `find_dotenv` (start hit / nested dirs / nearest-wins precedence / depth cap / cwd default / none-when-absent), `load_dotenv` (sets missing / preserves pre-set when `override=False` / overrides on `override=True` / skips empty values / ignores comments and blanks), `load_dotenv_walk_up` (no-env empty / idempotent / worktree-shaped tree).

### Changed (S-0049 ŌĆö walk-up `.env` loader; Issue #8 closed)
- [`engine/tools/check_target.py`](tools/check_target.py) `main()` ŌĆö calls `load_dotenv_walk_up()` before argparse so `_check_migration_applied` sees `SUPABASE_DB_URL`.
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) `main()` ŌĆö same wiring before argparse so `_read_graph_from_db` sees `SUPABASE_DB_URL` and the graph audit engages.
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) graph audit ŌĆö psycopg `ImportError` flipped from hard-fail to soft-skip (records `graph_audit_skipped` + stderr note). Pre-S-0049 the hard-fail was correct because `SUPABASE_DB_URL` being set was an explicit user commitment to having psycopg. Post-S-0049, the walk-up loader auto-loads the URL in any reachable-`.env` context including pre-commit's system-Python invocation (no psycopg there). Audit-skip is the right disposition for that case; the stderr note flags the gap if a user *intended* the audit.
- [`HANDOFF.md`](../HANDOFF.md) ŌĆö would-be-S-0049 routine fire's HANDOFF entry gains a `**Resolved:** S-0049 (commit 21285f8)` line per the disposition discipline.

### Fixed (S-0049 ŌĆö walk-up `.env` loader; Issue #8 closed)
- **GitHub Issue #8 closed.** Backlog 3 ŌåÆ 2 (only upstream MemPalace #1, #2 remain). Live verification: `check_target.py --task-id P5-01a` from this worktree (no local `.env`, `SUPABASE_DB_URL` unset in shell) correctly queried the DB and reported `migration_applied` FAIL with "migration 0011_seed_epistemology_part1 not in schema_migrations" ŌĆö i.e., URL was loaded via walk-up, DB was queried, migration is correctly absent (Phase 5 hasn't started). `validate.py` ran 30 checks (was 23) ŌĆö graph audit engaged. Pre-commit hook still works correctly under system Python via the soft-skip path. pytest 576/576 (was 562; +14 new). User can resume `paideia-engine-loop` Routine in Hourly mode.

### Added (S-0048 ŌĆö GitHub Issues backlog cleanup; 5 issues closed)
- [`engine/tools/check_settings_sync.py`](tools/check_settings_sync.py) ŌĆö **new pre-commit guard** (per Issue #5). Hard-fails any commit from a worktree where main's `.claude/settings.json` differs from the worktree's tracked copy AND the worktree's copy is not staged for the current commit. Resolves the silent-no-op vector that hit S-0046 (harness redirected the worktree Write to main's copy; `git status` from the worktree saw no diff; close commit shipped without the deliverable). Detects worktree via `git rev-parse --git-common-dir` + `realpath` mirroring the pattern in `engine/tools/scrub_env.sh:67-72`. Silent no-op when not in a worktree or when files match. Exit codes: 0 synced/not-applicable, 1 divergent-not-staged hard-fail, 2 tool error. Wired into `engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit` after the routine-mode scope-check.
- [`engine/tools/test_check_settings_sync.py`](tools/test_check_settings_sync.py) ŌĆö **12 tests.** Three layers: pure-function (`files_differ`), `main()` integration with monkeypatched helpers (no-conflict / in-sync / divergent-not-staged hard-fails / divergent-staged passes / missing-worktree-file treated-as-divergent), real-git integration (`detect_worktree` + `is_staged` against tmp_path repos with worktree subprocess + a real-worktree end-to-end). All 12 pass under venv Python 3.12 and system Python 3.9.
- [`engine/tools/check_session_conflict.py`](tools/check_session_conflict.py) ŌĆö **new boot-time guard** (per Issue #3). Detects when `register_state.json` says `current_status: in_progress` before the eager-claim ritual runs. Three dispositions: exit 0 no-conflict (closed/absent or current.json absent or unparseable), exit 1 recent collision (<1h) or ambiguous mid-window (1hŌĆō24h), exit 2 stale (>24h, recovery candidate). Configurable windows via `--recent-window-seconds` / `--stale-window-seconds`. Wired into `engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh` (informational; hook always exits 0) and `/start-engine` step 4b + session-build-lifecycle.md step 5b (refusal point for the AI).
- [`engine/tools/test_check_session_conflict.py`](tools/test_check_session_conflict.py) ŌĆö **16 tests.** Cover `parse_started_at` (Z-suffix, `+00:00`, malformed ŌåÆ None), every `check()` disposition (no-register / closed / in-progress + various age windows / future-dated clock-skew / Z-suffix parsing / custom windows), `main()` integration with `--repo-root` and `--quiet`. Real e2e against in-flight S-0048 confirmed correct identification (14-min-old session as recent collision, exit 1, LOUD surface).
- [`engine/tools/setup_env.py`](tools/setup_env.py) ŌĆö **new one-time `.env` setup helper** (per Issue #7). Reads `.env.example` to discover canonical keys, reads `.env` to preserve existing values, prompts only for missing/empty keys, validates `SUPABASE_DB_URL` with a real `psycopg.connect()` + `SELECT version()`, writes `.env` atomically (write-tmp + rename) with 0600 permissions. Idempotent ŌĆö re-running with all values populated prints "all set" and exits. Replaces "user manually pastes the URL into .env once, ever" with a guided one-time setup that validates as it goes; subsequent routine fires read the populated `.env` directly.
- [`engine/tools/test_setup_env.py`](tools/test_setup_env.py) ŌĆö **15 tests.** Cover `parse_env_example` (simple / no-comments / multi-line comment block), `parse_env` (basic / whitespace-strip / value-with-equals / blank-and-comment-ignored / no-equals-ignored), `write_env_atomic` (round-trip / 0600 permission / overwrite-existing), `determine_blocks` (all-populated short-circuit / missing-key prompts / empty-value-prompts / skipped-value-stays-empty).
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) ŌĆö **two new boot surfaces.** (1) Concurrent-session collision check: invokes `check_session_conflict.py` after the cadence-trigger surface; surfaces stderr at exit 1/2; hook always exits 0 per its "never blocks" design. (2) `.env` onboarding pointer: emits a LOUD surface when `engine/session/auto_target.json` is present AND `.env` is missing `SUPABASE_DB_URL`, naming the exact `setup_env.py` command. Goes silent the moment `.env` carries the URL. `log_ok` telemetry gains `conflict=<status>` and `env_pointer=<status>` fields.
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) ŌĆö **new "Editing settings.json from a worktree" subsubsection** under "Harness permission allowlist" documenting the cp procedure that the new pre-commit guard's stderr message points at. The guard is a backstop for any session that forgets the cp.

### Changed (S-0048 ŌĆö GitHub Issues backlog cleanup; 5 issues closed)
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) ŌĆö **"Harness permission allowlist" subsection rewritten end-to-end** (per Issue #6). New operational stance: routine sessions run in **Auto** permission mode; project-level mechanical safeguards (`check_routine_scope.py --plan/--staged`, master-plan-integrity, `audit_handoff_dispositions.py`, validate.py soft-warns, eager-claim atomic protocol) are the load-bearing anti-rogue layer. Why the S-0046 allowlist approach didn't generalize: the AI inside a routine session naturally uses compound Bash forms (`cmd1; cmd2`, `cmd && cmd`) and the harness matches the *whole* compound command against patterns rather than the leading prefix ŌĆö pattern proliferation never converges. New trade-off table enumerating what Auto mode permits vs what each project safeguard prevents (for routine-task work, edits outside scope_lock, master-plan revisions, destructive ops, HANDOFF disposition, gh issue create, arbitrary new Bash). Allowlist stays in `.claude/settings.json` for interactive `/start-engine` sessions where Default + human-in-the-loop adds value. The S-0046 same-commit pairing rule is retired.
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) ŌĆö **"Mechanical safeguard" subsection flipped from "planned, not yet landed" to "landed at S-0048 per Issue #3"** (per Issue #3 closure). Names `check_session_conflict.py`'s three dispositions and the two wire-points (session-start hook + slash command boot procedure).
- [`engine/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) ŌĆö **new step 5b** before the eager-claim ritual: run `check_session_conflict.py`, refuse on exit 1 (recent collision or ambiguous mid-window), offer auto-recovery on exit 2 (stale).
- [`.claude/commands/start-engine.md`](../.claude/commands/start-engine.md) ŌĆö **new step 4b** matching the session-build-lifecycle addition.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) ŌĆö **new settings.json sync check section** invoking `check_settings_sync.py` after the routine-mode scope-check. Hard-fails commits from a worktree where main vs worktree `.claude/settings.json` differ AND the worktree's copy isn't staged.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) ŌĆö **mechanization-list bullet for "Routine-mode harness permission allowlist" rewritten** to match the Auto-mode-supersedes-allowlist stance per Issue #6.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) ŌĆö **new posture bullet** under "Posture vs machinery" ŌåÆ "postures held by AI discipline" naming the operating policy for context-pressure monitoring (Issue #4 closed as intractable). Live transcript-token measurement is infrastructurally blocked (Claude Code does not expose the in-progress transcript path to hooks); prior-archive telemetry is too noisy a proxy; tiktoken estimates are imprecise even at shutdown. User policy: manually monitor context load during routine review; sessions archived with `transcript_token_pct >= 0.70` get post-hoc review pass.
- [`README.md`](../README.md) ŌĆö **"Setup for a fresh clone" section** adds the `python3 engine/tools/setup_env.py` step plus dashboard URL guidance (where to find `SUPABASE_DB_URL`, what to do if the dashboard masks the password).
- [`engine/operations/seed-chunked-authoring.md`](operations/seed-chunked-authoring.md) ŌĆö **new "One-time setup of `SUPABASE_DB_URL`" subsubsection** under "Validator skip behavior" documenting the helper + the dashboard-only nature of the DB password.
- [`.claude/settings.json`](../.claude/settings.json) ŌĆö **three new allowlist entries** for the new tools (`check_settings_sync.py`, `check_session_conflict.py`, `setup_env.py`).

### Fixed (S-0047 ŌĆö Settings.json desync patch; lands S-0046's missing deliverable)
- [`.claude/settings.json`](../.claude/settings.json) ŌĆö **the actual 60+ pattern allowlist extension committed in git for the first time.** S-0046's close commit (2c5da6c) shipped the companion documentation (routine-mode-operations.md subsection, CLAUDE.md mechanization-list bullet, STATE.md and ENGINE_LOG entries) but missed this file because the harness redirected the in-session Write to main repo's `.claude/settings.json` (where the harness reads from) while git tracked the worktree's stale copy. The desync was invisible to `git status` from the worktree (no diff) and the close commit landed looking complete despite the deliverable being functionally absent from git. S-0047's one-line fix: `cp <main>/.claude/settings.json <worktree>/.claude/settings.json && git add && git commit`. Pairs with the routine-mode-operations.md "Harness permission allowlist" subsection that landed in S-0046 documenting the rule.
- **GitHub Issue #5 filed** per ADR 0048 issue-discipline: `bug` ŌĆö the systemic gap (harness Write to `.claude/settings.json` from a worktree redirects to main; git tracks the worktree's local copy). Proposes (A) pre-commit hook check that compares main vs worktree settings.json and hard-fails on diff-not-staged, (B) auto-sync on session boot, (C) document the asymmetry in routine-mode-operations.md. Recommendation in Issue body: A + C. Out of S-0047 scope (the fixup is single-deliverable).

### Changed (S-0046 ŌĆö Routine-mode harness permission allowlist patch)
- [`.claude/settings.json`](../.claude/settings.json) ŌĆö **`permissions.allow` extended** to cover the routine procedure's complete Bash command surface. Pre-S-0046 the file held only the main-repo lifecycle git commands (FF-merge, push, log, status, rev-parse, fetch, diff). Post-S-0046 it covers: engine python tools (every `engine/tools/*.py` script invokable via `python3` with any args ŌĆö `check_target`, `check_routine_scope`, `validate`, `scan_context_telemetry`, `audit_handoff_dispositions`, `scan_issue_*`, `scan_orphans`, `health_check`, `probe_*`, `parse_structural_reference`, `audit_side_discoveries`); worktree-side git lifecycle (`add/commit/rm/mv/status/diff/log/rev-parse/fetch/show/ls-files/pull --ff-only origin main/config --get`); test/lint stack (`pytest`, `ruff`, `mypy` direct and via `python3 -m`); GitHub Issues path (`gh issue create/list/view/close/comment` plus `gh label list`); Supabase migration tooling (`supabase db push/migration new/migration list/migration repair`); hook scripts (`bash engine/tools/hooks/*.sh`); shell utilities (`date`, `ls`, `cat` of session files, `head/tail/wc/grep/rg/find . -name`); MemPalace CLI (`mempalace search/status/list-drawers/add-drawer/diary read/diary write`); `source engine/tools/scrub_env.sh`. Closes the S-0044 gap where the foundation shipped a load-bearing assumption ("we'll lean on the allowlist") without authoring the allowlist; the first manual routine fire after S-0045 master plan deadlocked at the boot procedure's very first Bash invocation (`python3 engine/tools/check_target.py` for the target-met check).
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) ŌĆö **new "Harness permission allowlist" subsection** placed after "Mixing interactive and routine sessions". Documents the executability vs. correctness layer distinction (harness allowlist vs. project-level scope-lock per ADR 0051); the S-0044 lesson; the rule that adding a new Bash invocation to the routine procedure REQUIRES a paired allowlist entry in the same commit; the verification path (manual routine fire + boot procedure walk); the recovery path when a routine deadlocks (deny ŌåÆ identify pattern ŌåÆ patch allowlist ŌåÆ re-fire). Routine UI configuration table updated: "Ask permissions: Default" entry's Notes column now references `.claude/settings.json` (project-scope, tracked) instead of `.claude/settings.local.json` (gitignored).
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) ŌĆö **mechanization-list bullet added for the harness permission allowlist** as the executability layer that complements ADR 0051's scope-lock (correctness layer). Names the same-commit pairing rule.

### Added (S-0045 ŌĆö Phase 5 master plan; routine-mode dispatches against auto_target.json)
- [`product/adr/0052-phase-5-philosophy-subdomain-decomposition.md`](../product/adr/0052-phase-5-philosophy-subdomain-decomposition.md) ŌĆö **new product ADR.** Phase 5 decomposes into 9 subject subdomains (epistemology, metaphysics, logic, ethics, political philosophy, aesthetics, philosophy of mind, philosophy of language, philosophy of science) plus 3 operational tasks (service nodes, cross-bridges, closeout). Class-boundary admit-criterion governs future readmission (top-level coverage in SEP/Routledge browse categories AND graph-shape distinctness from existing 9 subdomains AND non-trivial concept inventory at the granularity principle). Out of scope, deferred: philosophy of religion (cosmological-argument-shaped concepts fold into metaphysics for this MVP); history of philosophy as separate subdomain (per ADR 0008, thinkers are not nodes; historical concepts surface across the 9 subdomains via cross-bridges). Adjudication closed material divergence between canonical build_plan/ROADMAP list (6 subjects, missing logic/political/aesthetics) and post-S-0044 STATE.md text (8 subjects, missing philosophy of language and standalone services).
- [`engine/build_readiness/phase_5.md`](build_readiness/phase_5.md) ŌĆö **new gate report covering full Phase 5 batch.** Authored by S-0045 master plan session per ADR 0040 + ADR 0051 (master plan IS the gate session for Phase 5). 7 Tier 1 entries (subdomain decomposition, task pre-splitting, max_sessions, depends_on graph, cross_domain_dependency deferral, closeout criteria, paused state); 8 Tier 2 entries (migration ranges, confidence_level composition, soft-warn recalibrations, scope_lock shape, criteria shape, depends_on encoding, adversarial reconnaissance, source-acquisition); 7 Tier 3 forward-pointers (rollback verification, cross_domain_dependency predicate, rigor_score calibration, soft-warn thresholds, adversarial-triage prompt template, mid-session context-pressure signal, philosophy of religion readmission). Every Tier 1/2 decision cites source-document line(s) per ADR 0040.
- [`engine/session/auto_target.json`](session/auto_target.json) ŌĆö **new executable contract.** `target_id: T-PHASE-5`, `goal`, `paused: false`, `max_sessions: 18`, `max_wall_clock_hours: 96`, 16 explicit tasks. Subdomains pre-split at master-plan time per `auto_target.schema.md:149` ("Break work into session-sized tasks"): epistemology core/specialized (P5-01a/b), metaphysics core/specialized (P5-02a/b), ethics metaethics+normative/applied (P5-04a/b), philosophy of mind core/consciousness-specialized (P5-07a/b). Single tasks: logic (P5-03), political philosophy (P5-05), aesthetics (P5-06), philosophy of language (P5-08), philosophy of science (P5-09), service nodes (P5-10), cross-bridges (P5-11), closeout (P5-12). Per-task tight `scope_lock.allowed_paths` matching the migration sub-range plus PREDICATE_MANIFEST.md and ROUTING.md. `criteria` are objective, runnable: `migration_applied` for the first migration in the task's range plus `validate_passes` for subdomain tasks; closeout uses `adr_status` + `file_exists` + `validate_passes`. `depends_on` graph: P5-01a anchor; b-halves depend on their a-halves; subjects parallel-eligible after P5-01a; cross-bridges blocks on all 9 subjects + services; closeout blocks on cross-bridges.
- **GitHub Issue #4 filed** per ADR 0048 issue-discipline: `enhancement` ŌĆö Mid-session context-pressure signal for routine-mode sessions. Routine sessions have no live context-pressure detection (CLAUDE.md budget percentages are AI posture, not machinery; `scan_context_telemetry.py` runs only at shutdown; auto-compact fires too late at ~95%). Out of S-0045 scope; routed to backlog. S-0045 engineers around the gap by sizing tasks pre-execution per the schema's discipline.

- [`engine/tools/check_target.py`](tools/check_target.py) ŌĆö **fix-in-context.** `_check_validate_passes` was treating validate.py exit 1 as fail; per `auto_target.schema.md` (validate_passes section), criterion passes iff zero hard-fails. validate.py main() exits 1 whenever any soft-warn fires; the persistent `issue_collision` soft-warns from open Issues #1/#2/#3/#4 keyword-matching every routine session would have blocked all routine `validate_passes` criteria. Fixed: criterion now passes when validate.py exits 0 OR 1; only exit 2 (hard fails) is fail. Updated docstring explains the three-exit-code semantic.

All three exercise `_check_validate_passes` against monkeypatched `subprocess.run` with the three documented validate.py exit codes. Suite rises 30 ŌåÆ 33 tests for check_target; full pytest suite 516 ŌåÆ 519.


- [`engine/adr/0051-routine-mode-and-engine-loop.md`](adr/0051-routine-mode-and-engine-loop.md) ŌĆö **new engine ADR.** Third session mode alongside exploration and build: unattended cadence-driven Claude Code Routines that read `engine/session/auto_target.json`, pick the next eligible task, run plan-then-scope-check, execute or exit gracefully without claiming. Two-layer architecture: master plan session (interactive, `/start-engine`) authors the target contract; engine loop (unattended, `/start-routine`) executes it. They share only the eager-claim ritual; everything else (boot procedure, scope rules, commit posture, permission model, shutdown logic) is mode-specific. Six-layer defense in depth: boot-time scope-check on the session plan, commit-time scope-check on staged files (task `scope_lock` Ōł¬ operational allowlist), master-plan integrity hard-fail on non-status diffs to `auto_target.json`, existing `audit_handoff_dispositions.py`, new `routine_issue_spam` soft-warn at >3 issues per session, new `routine_no_target_reference` soft-warn for plan-target alignment. **Paperclip rejected** (Anthropic April-2026 third-party-orchestration policy excludes from subscription coverage; Paperclip GitHub #1163 and #3270 confirm `claude_local` adapter's subscription path is incompatible with unattended dispatch). Reasoning preserved in ADR 0051 Alternatives Considered. Phase 5 epistemology build-readiness gate (twice-displaced) reframed: the gate report at `engine/build_readiness/phase_5.md` is now authored by the Phase 5 master plan session (S-0045+) as part of producing the `auto_target.json` contract.
- [`engine/operations/routine-mode-operations.md`](operations/routine-mode-operations.md) ŌĆö **new Layer 1 ops doc** (reference-shaped per ADR 0044). Target file schema, master plan session procedure, routine boot procedure, criterion catalog, scope-lock model, mixing interactive and routine sessions, troubleshooting.
- [`engine/session/auto_target.schema.md`](session/auto_target.schema.md) ŌĆö **new schema reference doc.** Top-level fields (`target_id`, `goal`, `paused`, `max_sessions`, `max_wall_clock_hours`, `tasks`); per-task fields (`id`, `name`, `depends_on`, `criteria`, `scope_lock`, `status`, `blocked_reason`); five criterion types (`migration_applied`, `validate_passes`, `adr_status`, `file_exists`, `predicate`) with shape examples; complete Phase 5 sketch example.
- [`engine/tools/check_target.py`](tools/check_target.py) ŌĆö **new tool.** Predicate runner for target file criteria. Five criterion types ship at landing; predicate-registry escape hatch for non-standard criteria. CLI: `--target`, `--task-id`, `--json`. 30 unit tests.
- [`engine/tools/check_routine_scope.py`](tools/check_routine_scope.py) ŌĆö **new tool.** Three enforcement points: plan-vs-scope (boot-time, `--plan`), staged-vs-scope (commit-time, `--staged`), master-plan integrity (commit-time, automatic when `auto_target.json` is staged). Segment-aware glob matching (`*` segment-bounded, `**` cross-segment). Operational allowlist constants. CLI: `--plan PATH`, `--staged`, `--task-id`, `--target`, `--repo-root`. 40 unit tests.
- [`.claude/commands/start-routine.md`](../.claude/commands/start-routine.md) ŌĆö **new slash command.** Architecturally distinct from `/start-engine` per S-0044 user direction: bolting routine-mode into `/start-engine` conflated five differences (boot, scope, commit, permission, shutdown). Two clean entry points share only the eager-claim ritual.
- [`.claude/skills/routine-mode-lifecycle/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/routine-mode-lifecycle/SKILL.md) ŌĆö **new recipe-shaped Skill** (per ADR 0044). Mirrors the routine boot procedure in routine-mode-operations.md. `disable-model-invocation: true` ŌĆö invoked deliberately, not auto-fired.
- 3 new test files: `test_check_target.py` (30 tests), `test_check_routine_scope.py` (40 tests), `test_validate_routine_mode.py` (12 tests). 82 new tests total. Full suite 516 passing.
- **GitHub Issue #3 filed** per ADR 0048 issue-discipline: `/start-engine` boot procedure should detect `current_status: in_progress` with a recent `started_at` and refuse to claim mid-routine. Out of S-0044 scope (would expand the session beyond declared scope per ADR 0049); routed to Issue. Surfaced when user asked "What if I start a manual interactive session while routine mode sessions are running?" ŌĆö apparatus assumes one active session at a time and would corrupt state on collision. Procedural workaround documented in routine-mode-operations.md "Mixing interactive and routine sessions" (set `paused: true`, wait for in-flight to close, then start interactive).

### Changed (S-0044 ŌĆö Routine-mode foundation)
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) ŌĆö **new `validate_routine_mode()` function** with two soft-warn categories: `routine_no_target_reference` (current_plan.md exists but doesn't mention active task's id or name; suggests routine session drifted from target) and `routine_issue_spam` (>3 GitHub issues created since session's `started_at`; defense-in-depth against confused-session containment; legitimate fix-this-many findings ride through). Both no-op when not in routine-mode. Wired into default-mode dispatch. Default-mode validator check count rises 21 ŌåÆ 23.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) ŌĆö **new routine-mode scope-check section.** Always-invoked when `engine/session/auto_target.json` exists; the tool itself detects routine-mode (target + current_plan.md + in_progress task) and exits 0 silently when not applicable. Hard-fails staged out-of-scope paths AND non-status diffs to `auto_target.json` from routine commits.
- [`engine/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) ŌĆö **routine-mode reframed as a separate lifecycle**, not a branch of /start-engine's boot procedure. Notes /start-routine + routine-mode-lifecycle Skill as the architecturally distinct path. They share only the eager-claim ritual.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) ŌĆö **third session mode** (`routine`) added alongside exploration and build, with explicit posture for scope_lock invariance, operational allowlist, `gh issue create` authorization, HANDOFF additions, and master-plan-revision-via-HANDOFF rule. Mechanization-list bullet added for ADR 0051 routine-mode scope-lock and master-plan integrity. Topical pointer added for routine-mode-operations.md. Note about four-skills now (with `routine-mode-lifecycle` joining the existing three).
- [`engine/STATE.md`](STATE.md) ŌĆö **Paperclip integration entry rewritten** as "Rejected at S-0044, superseded by ADR 0051" with the cost-calculus rationale and the conditions under which Paperclip becomes a reasonable revisit.
- [`engine/operations/README.md`](operations/README.md) ŌĆö `routine-mode-operations.md` added to Session protocol section.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) ŌĆö index extended with ADR 0051; engine ADR count rises 16 ŌåÆ 17 (corrected count line that had drifted to 15 pre-S-0044); project total 50 ŌåÆ 51.
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) (lines 1905-1906) ŌĆö **pre-existing unused `# type: ignore` paired** for psycopg imports as `# type: ignore[import-not-found,unused-ignore]`. Mid-session fix-in-context per CLAUDE.md ŌĆö paired form satisfies both the pre-commit hook's mypy invocation (which can't see venv-installed psycopg in some subprocess contexts) and standalone post-cache-clear mypy (which can). Pre-existing tech debt that mypy cache had been masking at S-0043 close.

### Added (S-0043 ŌĆö Project venv with hook PATH wiring; mempalace migration; tiktoken activation)
- [`engine/adr/0050-project-venv-and-hook-path-wiring.md`](adr/0050-project-venv-and-hook-path-wiring.md) ŌĆö **new engine ADR.** Project-local Python venv at `<main_repo>/.venv/`, managed by `uv`, pinned to Python 3.12 via tracked `.python-version`. Hook scripts resolve `python3` and other tool entry points via a sourcing-time PATH prepend in `engine/tools/scrub_env.sh` ŌĆö worktree-local `.venv/` preferred, main repo's `.venv/` fallback. Single intervention point: PATH preservation across `scrubbed_env()` (per ADR 0045) propagates through every nested invocation, so `validate.py` and all eight current Python invocation sites pick up venv tools without per-script edits. Three previously implicit deps now explicitly pinned in `engine/tools/requirements.txt`: `chromadb` (was carried only by user-scope incidental install), `tiktoken` (activates the accurate-tokenizer branch in `scan_context_telemetry.py` per ADR 0049), `mempalace` (migrated from user-scope system Python 3.9 ŌåÆ project venv 3.12, addressing recurring Python-version issues with the tool). MemPalace upgrade 3.3.3 ŌåÆ 3.3.4 verified at S-0043 against Issues #1 and #2: Issue #1 reproduces verbatim (wing-filtered search "Internal error"); Issue #2 wing-derivation behavior changed (`wing_<last-token>` instead of full encoded path) but per-worktree fragmentation persists and the new `wing_paideia` is distinct from the documented bare `paideia` wing.
- [`.python-version`](../.python-version) ŌĆö **new tracked file** at main repo root. Pins Python to `3.12`. uv reads this when creating venvs.

### Changed (S-0043 ŌĆö Project venv migration)
- [`engine/tools/scrub_env.sh`](tools/scrub_env.sh) ŌĆö **adds sourcing-time PATH-prepend behavior** alongside the existing `scrub_git_env` function. Resolves worktree root and main-repo root via `git rev-parse --show-toplevel` and `git rev-parse --git-common-dir` (with `realpath` normalization for the relative-path return case); prefers worktree-local `.venv/bin/`, falls back to main repo's; idempotent via `case ":$PATH:"` substring guard; silent no-op when neither venv exists or when sourced outside a git repo. Header comment expanded to document both responsibilities (scrub + wire) and motivating failures (S-0033 GIT_DIR leak; S-0043 system-Python coupling).
- [`engine/tools/requirements.txt`](tools/requirements.txt) ŌĆö **three new explicit pins.** `chromadb>=0.5.0` (closes silent-dependency gap; previously imported by `probe_palace.py` but not declared). `tiktoken>=0.7.0` (activates `tiktoken-o200k_base` tokenizer in `scan_context_telemetry.py` per ADR 0049; archives going forward carry accurate token counts rather than `chars-div-4-fallback`). `mempalace>=3.3.3` (migrates mempalace from user-scope into project venv per ADR 0050 decision).
- [`.mcp.json`](../.mcp.json) ŌĆö **mempalace-mcp command path updated** to `<main_repo>/.venv/bin/mempalace-mcp`. Local-only edit (file is gitignored). Hook wrapper at `engine/tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh` resolves mempalace via PATH (now venv-prepended) and needs no edits.
- [`engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`](operations/mempalace-operations.md) ŌĆö **Known issues section updated for 3.3.4 verification.** Issue #1 entry adds re-verification note (bug reproduces verbatim in 3.3.4). Issue #2 entry rewritten to describe the 3.3.4 `_wing_from_transcript_path` `rsplit("-", 1)[-1]` behavior change and the new `wing_paideia` vs. bare `paideia` wing distinction.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) ŌĆö index extended with ADR 0050; engine ADR count rises 15 ŌåÆ 16; project total 49 ŌåÆ 50.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) ŌĆö mechanization-list bullet added for project venv + ADR 0050.
- [`engine/session/current.json`](session/current.json) ŌĆö S-0043's own `current.json` written at eager-claim with `declared_scope` (including `phase: NA-engine-apparatus` operational marker) per ADR 0049.

### Added (S-0042 ŌĆö Engine apparatus improvements: HANDOFF/Issues split + multi-axis health-check + scope-lock + telemetry)
- [`engine/adr/0048-handoff-narrowing-and-github-issues-for-cross-session-deferrals.md`](adr/0048-handoff-narrowing-and-github-issues-for-cross-session-deferrals.md) ŌĆö **new engine ADR.** Narrows HANDOFF.md to session-internal handoffs (partial-closure, in-flight recovery, atomic ownership transfer); routes cross-session deferrals to GitHub Issues with a six-label taxonomy (`bug`, `enhancement`, `tech-debt`, `cleanup`, `health-check-finding`, `upstream`) plus one priority label (`priority:urgent`). Boot-time backlog visibility via `scan_issue_backlog.py` + `session-start.sh` integration; scope-collision detection via `scan_issue_collisions.py` + `validate.py` integration. Closes the cleanup-treadmill failure mode the planning thread named: every HANDOFF entry creates implicit "next session must address this" pressure; Issues sit silently in a labelled backlog with cleanup-batch workflow.
- [`engine/adr/0049-scope-lock-at-boot-and-descope-reorder-audit-at-shutdown.md`](adr/0049-scope-lock-at-boot-and-descope-reorder-audit-at-shutdown.md) ŌĆö **new engine ADR.** Three coupled mechanisms: (1) `declared_scope` field at boot in `current.json`; (2) scope-delivery audit at shutdown with structured `{delivered, user_confirmed_changes, explanation}` field; (3) session-end context telemetry via transcript tokenization (closes the context-state opacity failure mode ŌĆö Claude Code does not expose context usage to running code, but the transcript JSONL is the available proxy). Three new validator soft-warns: `empty_declared_scope`, `phase_mismatch_declared_scope`, `scope_delivery_non_yes`. Multi-session scope-erosion signal at next boot. Build-readiness gate gains a no-descoping-or-reordering clause closing the S-0037 phase-5-before-4.5 vector.
- [`engine/operations/issue-discipline.md`](operations/issue-discipline.md) ŌĆö **new Layer 1 ops doc.** HANDOFF-vs-Issue decision rule (immediacy + ownership + session-context-dependency criteria); label taxonomy with semantic definitions; Issue body shape requiring an "Affected files" section that the collision-detection scanner consumes; cleanup-batch workflow; boot-time visibility surfaces; scope-collision detection wiring.
- [`engine/build_readiness/engine_apparatus_improvements_s0042.md`](build_readiness/engine_apparatus_improvements_s0042.md) ŌĆö **new build-readiness gate report.** Compressed gate execution per ADR 0040 (planning thread carried steps 1-5 conversationally with 3 parallel Explore agents + user-directed Tier 1 resolution on the orphan-definition lens correction). Cold-review pass against citations applied four sharpenings (test count made dynamic; T2-A regex aligned with existing pattern style; T2-F phase example clarified; T2-G ambiguity resolved with structured field shape).
- [`engine/tools/scan_issue_backlog.py`](tools/scan_issue_backlog.py) ŌĆö **new tool.** Wraps `gh issue list`, counts by canonical label set, surfaces FYI line at every boot or LOUD attention block when `priority:urgent` count > 0. Best-effort: `gh` failure ŌåÆ stderr note + exit 0. 16 unit tests.
- [`engine/tools/scan_issue_collisions.py`](tools/scan_issue_collisions.py) ŌĆö **new tool.** Reads `current.json`'s `declared_scope` (with `working_on` fallback for pre-ADR-0049 sessions), tokenizes for keywords (lowercase, drop stopwords + short tokens), collects staged-files paths, queries open Issues, soft-warns per match. Word-boundary matching avoids spurious hits. 25 unit tests.
- [`engine/tools/scan_orphans.py`](tools/scan_orphans.py) ŌĆö **new tool.** Five-axis multi-dimensional dead-weight scanner: reference-count (<3 inbound refs), last-mod-age (only 1 substantive commit AND inbound-refs below 5-ref ceiling), register-emptiness (markdown table headers with no data rows), ops-doc-uncited (engine/operations/*.md with 0 archive citations in last 20 sessions), stale-pending-marker (decide-trigger / decide-before / open decide-by markers in low-commit-count files). Output: per-candidate annotated markdown for the audit's "is this file doing the work it was created to do?" triage. Verified on live repo: surfaces `ideation.md` (register-empty), `sub-agent-validation.md` and `tools-sweep-worktrees.md` (multi-axis), `prep-paideia-prompt-pack.md` (stale-marker). 18 unit tests.
- [`engine/tools/scan_context_telemetry.py`](tools/scan_context_telemetry.py) ŌĆö **new tool.** Auto-detects session transcript at `~/.claude/projects/<encoded-project-path>/<session-id>.jsonl` (most-recently-modified .jsonl), tokenizes with tiktoken `o200k_base` when installed (chars/4 fallback otherwise), writes `transcript_token_estimate` + `transcript_token_pct` + `tokenizer_used` to `current.json` for the cross-session "running too long / too short / high variance" judgment in the rewritten health-check Session-load trend section. 14 unit tests.
- **GitHub Issues #1 + #2 filed** as the seed `bug + upstream` exercise of the new tracker per ADR 0048: [#1](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/1) wing-filtered search throws Internal error, [#2](https://github.com/StarshipSuperjam/paideia/issues/2) hook auto-capture creates one wing per worktree. Both upstream in mempalace 3.3.3 (not in-project remediable). Documentation cross-references the S-0040 HANDOFF entries (Resolved) and the workaround at `engine/operations/mempalace-operations.md`.
- 7 GitHub label definitions confirmed in the repo: `bug`, `enhancement`, `tech-debt`, `cleanup`, `health-check-finding`, `upstream`, `priority:urgent` per ADR 0048 taxonomy.
- 6 new test files: `test_scan_issue_backlog.py` (16 tests), `test_scan_issue_collisions.py` (25 tests), `test_scan_orphans.py` (18 tests), `test_scan_context_telemetry.py` (14 tests), `test_validate_scope_discipline.py` (14 tests), `test_validate_issue_collisions.py` (4 tests). 91 new tests total. Full suite 434 passing; ruff + mypy --strict clean.

### Changed (S-0042 ŌĆö Engine apparatus improvements)
- [`engine/tools/audit_handoff_dispositions.py`](tools/audit_handoff_dispositions.py) ŌĆö **fifth disposition pattern added** to `_VALID_DISPOSITION_PATTERNS`: `re.compile(r"^tracked-as-issue\s+#\d+$")`. Hint message extended with the fifth bullet. Module docstring updated to describe the pattern's purpose (cross-session deferral routed to Issues per ADR 0048). 2 new tests covering accept/reject cases.
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) ŌĆö **two new validation functions.** `validate_issue_collisions()` wraps `scan_issue_collisions.py` (new `issue_collision` soft-warn category; best-effort posture; missing-scanner soft-warn). `validate_scope_discipline()` reads `current.json` and emits up to three soft-warns: `empty_declared_scope`, `phase_mismatch_declared_scope` (substring + heuristic-token match against `build_plan/MANIFEST.md`; `NA-` prefix opts out for operational sessions), `scope_delivery_non_yes` (warn fires regardless of `user_confirmed_changes`; the warn is signal for cross-session aggregation). Both functions wired into default-mode dispatch. Default-mode validator check count rises 17 ŌåÆ 21.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) ŌĆö **two new boot surfaces.** Issues backlog visibility (between probe and persistent-warn surfaces): runs `scan_issue_backlog.py`, surfaces the FYI line at every boot. Multi-session scope-erosion signal (after persistent-warn surface): walks last 5 archives, counts `scope_delivery.delivered == false`, surfaces stderr block at 3-of-5 threshold. `log_ok` line gains `backlog=$BACKLOG_STATUS scope_non_yes=$SCOPE_NON_YES` telemetry fields.
- [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) ŌĆö **rewritten audit section** around the operative diagnostic question ("Is this thing doing the work it was created to do, or is it plumbing waiting for a function that never arrived?") borrowed verbatim from the user's framing during the S-0042 planning thread. New "Mechanical inputs" section names `scan_orphans.py` as the per-candidate triage feeder. Required: at least one non-obvious finding not on any mechanical scanner's output (forces meta-analysis on top of mechanical surfaces). New "Infrastructure-without-function" posture sharpens the dead-weight category ŌĆö each candidate ends with explicit disposition (retire / convert to active use / preserve with reason; "leave it for now" without naming why is itself the failure mode the audit exists to catch). Session-load trend section consumes the new ADR 0049 telemetry. Report template restructured to put the operative diagnostic + non-obvious finding sections first (the report is byproduct, not the deliverable).
- [`engine/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) ŌĆö **eager-claim ritual writes `declared_scope` and `scope_delivery: null`** in `current.json` template per ADR 0049. Validator soft-warns named.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) ŌĆö **two new steps.** Step 7a (scope-delivery audit per ADR 0049): explicit literal prompt to the AI (`Did you deliver the declared scope? If no, why not? Did anything get descoped, reordered, or deferred mid-session ŌĆö even with user confirmation?`) ŌåÆ structured field write to `current.json`. Step 7b (context telemetry per ADR 0049 cross-cutting addition): run `scan_context_telemetry.py` to capture transcript token estimate; fields travel with archive in step 9.
- [`engine/operations/build-readiness-gate.md`](operations/build-readiness-gate.md) ŌĆö **new step 4a no-descoping-or-reordering clause** per ADR 0049. The gate session itself is a descoping vector ŌĆö quietly trimming the chunk's deliverables or proposing reorderings ("Phase 5 before Phase 4.5") becomes the failure mode the scope-discipline machinery exists to catch. Any reduction OR reordering must be flagged to the user explicitly, not silently absorbed into the gate report.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) ŌĆö **four new soft-warn category entries** documenting `issue_collision`, `empty_declared_scope`, `phase_mismatch_declared_scope`, `scope_delivery_non_yes`.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) ŌĆö **"Default to fix-in-context" section updated** with the HANDOFF.md vs. GitHub Issues routing rule per ADR 0048 (`tracked-as-issue #<num>` is the fifth disposition form; cross-session deferrals default to Issues; HANDOFF.md narrows to session-internal handoffs).
- [`engine/operations/README.md`](operations/README.md) ŌĆö `issue-discipline.md` added to Session protocol section.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) ŌĆö index extended with ADRs 0048, 0049; engine ADR count rises 13 ŌåÆ 15; project total 47 ŌåÆ 49.

- All three Skill mirrors updated per ADR 0044 doc ŌåÆ skill direction: `session-build-lifecycle/SKILL.md` (declared_scope template), `session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md` (steps 7a + 7b), `build-readiness-gate/SKILL.md` (step 4a clause).

### Fixed (S-0041 ŌĆö Cadence-trigger overdue-catchup logic + second project health check)
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) ŌĆö **strict-modulo cadence trigger replaced with overdue-catchup tracking.** The S-0031 strict-modulo logic (`next_id mod cadence == 0`) was correct at the natural-cadence slot but introduced a silent-slide failure mode: when the cadence-aligned slot was consumed by user-directed work that deferred the audit (S-0040's slot was claimed for the deferred MemPalace wing-filter fix per S-0040's outcome_summary), the trigger silently slid forward by a full cadence ŌĆö the next firing would have landed at S-0050, a 19-session gap nearly 2x the configured cadence. The S-0041 boot caught the slide only because the user explicitly asked "this session is one past health check; why is it not engaging?" ŌĆö discovery surface was AI-noticing-after-being-prompted, not mechanical-detection. New logic: read `last_audit_session` from `register_state.json`, compute `slots_since = next_id - last_audit_session`, fire when `slots_since >= cadence`. Two surfaces: "due" at the natural-cadence slot, "overdue" at every later slot until the audit fires. Legacy fallback: when `last_audit_session` is absent (legacy `register_state.json`), revert to strict-modulo with a `last-audit-absent-falling-back-to-strict-modulo` log line so the regression is visible. Telemetry log_ok lines now carry `cadence-fires`, `cadence-mode`, `slots-since` instead of `cadence-remainder`.
- [`engine/session/register_state.json`](session/register_state.json) ŌĆö **schema gains `last_audit_session` field** (bootstrap value `S-0030`, the first audit) plus a `last_audit_session_field_history` array recording the field-addition rationale. The field is the canonical "audit happened" anchor that the SessionStart hook and validate.py's `health_check_overdue` check both consume.
- [`engine/tools/health_check.py`](tools/health_check.py) ŌĆö **`emit_report` bumps `register_state.json.last_audit_session`** to the report's session_id at non-dry-run report-emit time. New helper `bump_last_audit_session` performs the write with stderr-warning fallbacks (absent file, malformed JSON, write failure). Best-effort: failures do not poison the audit (the report is the durable artifact; the field bump is advisory tracking).
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) ŌĆö **new `health_check_overdue` soft-warn category** added to `validate_repo_structure()`. Defense-in-depth so a silently-failing SessionStart hook (the S-0033 / S-0034 vector pattern) cannot mask the slide. Fires when `(register_state.json.next_id - last_audit_session) > cadence` (strictly past the natural firing slot ŌĆö the natural slot is the hook's "due" surface, not an overdue condition). Skips quietly when `last_audit_session` is absent; the `checks_run` field still records the attempt. Default-mode validator check count rises 16 ŌåÆ 17.
- [`engine/tools/test_validate.py`](tools/test_validate.py) ŌĆö 4 new tests for `health_check_overdue`: overdue past natural slot fires; silent at the natural-cadence slot; silent when the field is absent (legacy schema); silent when slots_since is below cadence.
- [`engine/tools/test_health_check.py`](tools/test_health_check.py) ŌĆö 4 new tests for the field bump: emit_report bumps `last_audit_session` and preserves other fields; emit_report adds the field when absent (legacy ŌåÆ new-schema transition); dry-run skips the bump; absent register_state.json yields a stderr warning without poisoning the audit. 188 tests total still pass; ruff + mypy --strict clean.
- [`engine/adr/0022-periodic-project-health-checks.md`](adr/0022-periodic-project-health-checks.md) ŌĆö **Decision section + new Consequences amendment** recording the strict-modulo ŌåÆ overdue-catchup change at S-0041. Names the failure mode (silent slide of cadence-aligned slot consumption), the discovery surface (AI noticed only after user prompting), and the four-layer fix (register_state schema, hook, health_check.py, validate.py). Carriers updated list. Amendment-only per ADR 0036.
- [`engine/adr/0043-hook-architecture.md`](adr/0043-hook-architecture.md) ŌĆö **Consequences amended** with the S-0041 logic change. The strict-modulo fix this ADR committed at S-0031 is acknowledged as having been the right correction at the time but introducing the silent-slide mode; the S-0041 amendment supersedes the strict-modulo logic without superseding the ADR's contract (the cadence-trigger surface and the two-layer recording mechanization).
- [`engine/operations/health-check.md`](operations/health-check.md) ŌĆö **cadence-trigger logic prose updated** with the overdue-catchup formula, the "due" / "overdue" surface split, and a new "History of the cadence-trigger logic" subsection summarizing the S-0001 ŌåÆ S-0030 / S-0031 ŌåÆ S-0041 / S-0041 onward evolution. The validator's `health_check_overdue` defense-in-depth role is named.
- [`engine/operations/session-build-lifecycle.md`](operations/session-build-lifecycle.md) ŌĆö **Step 2 cadence-trigger prose rewritten** for overdue-catchup. The mirroring [`.claude/skills/session-build-lifecycle/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-build-lifecycle/SKILL.md) updated identically.
- [`.claude/commands/start-engine.md`](../.claude/commands/start-engine.md) ŌĆö **Step 2 prose updated** with the overdue-catchup formula and "due" / "overdue" surface text.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) ŌĆö **new `health_check_overdue` soft-warn category entry** under "Soft-warns (signal, not blocker)." Names the defense-in-depth role, the SessionStart hook's overlap, the silent-skip behavior when the field is absent, and the recovery procedure (run the audit script ŌĆö emit bumps the field ŌĆö or document explicit deferral).
- [`engine/scheduled_audits.json`](scheduled_audits.json) ŌĆö **S-0042 pushback/lesson tag adoption entry consumed.** The catch-up audit at S-0041 absorbed the check (Gaps section finding: zero adoption across S-0033 ŌåÆ S-0040). Entry moved from `audits` to a new `consumed_log` array preserving the audit trail. The file's `description` field updated to reflect the overdue-catchup logic per ADR 0022 amendment at S-0041.
- [`docs/health-checks/S-0041.md`](../docs/health-checks/S-0041.md) ŌĆö **second project health check report.** 5 mechanical (post-rewrite) + 13 manual observations across the five categories. Headline finding: the strict-modulo cadence-trigger silent-slide bug. Meta-finding: the audit was itself the case study of its own concern ŌĆö the AI authored the analysis at production quality but with too-narrow scope, then queued the recommended fixes for "future sessions" ŌĆö exactly the silent-deferral pattern CLAUDE.md "Default to fix-in-context" targets. The user pushed back twice ("STOP PUSHING THINGS OFF"; "Why is audit dead weight not scanning every folder? Why are they opt in only scans?"); both pushbacks drove inline fixes to the audit's recommendations + the audit's own scope. Net: 0 follow-up items carried forward to STATE.md.

### Fixed (S-0041 inline-fix batch ŌĆö every audit-recommended action plus user-surfaced fixes plus universal-scan rewrite)
- [`engine/scheduled_audits.json`](scheduled_audits.json) ŌĆö **S-0042 pushback/lesson tag adoption entry consumed.** The catch-up audit at S-0041 absorbed the check (Gaps section finding: zero adoption across S-0033 ŌåÆ S-0040). Entry moved from `audits` array to a new `consumed_log` array preserving the audit trail. The file's `description` field updated to reflect the overdue-catchup logic per ADR 0022 amendment at S-0041.
- [`engine/operations/mempalace-tagging-conventions.md`](operations/mempalace-tagging-conventions.md) ŌĆö **convention amendment for `pushback` and `lesson` capture.** Both tag definitions gain "Capture surface (added at S-0041)" paragraphs naming the explicit per-shutdown-step ask in `session-shutdown-sequence.md` step 7 as the canonical capture surface. The S-0041 audit measured zero adoption across 8 sessions of opportunity ŌĆö judgment-alone produced zero captures. The shutdown-step explicit yes/no ask makes the capture decision a structural surface, not a posture rule.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) ŌĆö **step 7 (diary write) gains a `pushback` / `lesson` capture check** paired with the diary write. Explicit yes/no asks for both tag candidates after the diary is written; if yes, capture via `mempalace_add_drawer` per the tag-definition shape (verbatim user framing + verbatim AI pushback + verbatim user acceptance + summary for `pushback`; failed approach + non-obvious reason + working fix + optional ADR pointers for `lesson`). The drawer lands before step 8 so capture is durable before archive.
- [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) ŌĆö **mirror of the new `pushback` / `lesson` capture step** per ADR 0036/0044 doc ŌåÆ skill propagation discipline.
- [`HANDOFF.md`](../HANDOFF.md) ŌĆö **all four entries dispositioned with explicit `Resolved:` lines + cross-refs.** (1) MemPalace capture mechanism (S-0001 ŌåÆ S-0002 work landed); (2) pre-commit + side-discovery audit (S-0032 ŌåÆ already Resolved at S-0033, no change); (3) worktree `core.bare=true` inheritance (S-0033 ŌåÆ resolved by [ADR 0045](adr/0045-shared-state-integrity-discipline.md) at S-0035 with cross-link to env-scrub mechanization); (4) stale-checkout vs halted-shutdown (post-S-0033 ŌåÆ resolved at S-0041 by adding the proposed sanity check to `session-shutdown-sequence.md` Recovery section + the skill mirror).
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) ŌĆö **Recovery section gains a "Pre-recovery sanity check" subsection** before the four recovery scenarios. Verifies the prior session's close commit isn't already on origin/main (the stale-checkout vs halted-shutdown discriminator from the post-S-0033 HANDOFF entry). The verification command, the asymmetry rationale, and the concrete trigger condition (`current_status: in_progress` AND `current.json` exists locally AND `git log origin/main` shows a `close S-<that-slot>` commit = stale checkout, NOT halted shutdown) all match the HANDOFF entry's proposal verbatim.
- [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) ŌĆö **mirror of the Recovery section "Pre-recovery sanity check" subsection** per ADR 0036/0044 doc ŌåÆ skill propagation discipline.
- [`product/docs/prep-paideia-prompt-pack.md`](../product/docs/prep-paideia-prompt-pack.md) ŌĆö **session dispositions retroactively applied** for all 14 prompts. Sessions 1-8 closed pre-Foundation (header re-dated). Session 9 closed at S-0004 (consumed by [ADR 0023](../product/adr/0023-engagement-depth-aggregation.md)) with cross-ref banner. Session 10 retired at S-0041 (superseded by Phase 7+ empirical verification of the V1 decay parameters once the learner model runs against real telemetry). Session 11 closed at S-0006 (consumed by [ADR 0025](../product/adr/0025-historical-maximum-tracking.md)) with cross-ref banner. Session 12 marked with explicit decide-trigger (first DeepTutor-divergence question OR first Phase 7 infrastructure session). Session 13 already closed at S-0016 (no change). Session 14 marked with explicit decide-trigger (first Phase 7 media-layer session). The file's "Updated 2026-04-29 during S-0001 foundation reorganization" header is replaced with an S-0041 status banner naming the file as historical reference + decide-trigger surface for the two open prompts. - [`engine/tools/sweep_worktrees.sh`](tools/sweep_worktrees.sh) ŌĆö **counter-bug fix.** The pipe-to-while pattern `git worktree list ... | while read -r WT_PATH; do ... REMOVED=$((REMOVED + 1)); done` ran the loop body in a subshell, so per-iteration increments to `REMOVED` and `SKIPPED` were lost; the final `[sweep] removed N, skipped K` line silently reported "removed 0, skipped 0" despite the actual removals. Fixed by switching to process substitution `done < <(git worktree list ...)` so the loop runs in the parent shell. Discovered when the S-0041 sweep removed 37 stale worktrees but the script's tally line showed zeros.
- **stale worktree sweep applied: 37 removed.** `engine/tools/sweep_worktrees.sh --apply` removed every claude/* worktree whose branch was fully merged into main and whose working tree was clean. Two worktrees survived: `frosty-dijkstra-484bac` (this session's worktree) and `flamboyant-sanderson-a81ba1` (dirty working tree). Worktree count: ~39 ŌåÆ 2 active.
- [`engine/tools/health_check.py`](tools/health_check.py) ŌĆö **universal-scan rewrite of audit_dead_weight + audit_bloat + audit_gaps.** Per the second user pushback ("Why is audit dead weight not scanning every folder? Why are they opt in only scans?"), the three audit categories are rewritten from opt-in directory-specific scans to universal scans over all `.md` files under `REPO_ROOT` (filesystem walk, not `git ls-files`, so the synthetic-repo test fixtures still work). New constants: `DEAD_WEIGHT_SKIP_PATH_PREFIXES` (`.claude/`, `engine/tools/test_fixtures/`, `engine/session/archive/`, `docs/health-checks/`) and `DEAD_WEIGHT_SKIP_NAMES` (per-file skip-list with structural reasons). New helpers: `_list_scanned_md_files()`, `_last_touched_session(path)`, `_count_inbound_citations(path, all_md)`. **audit_dead_weight** scans every tracked .md for staleness (no S-NNNN commit reference newer than `PRODUCT_DOC_STALE_SESSIONS = 20` sessions ago) and inbound-citation count (count of other .md files mentioning the file's name); files that hit either signal land in the report. **audit_bloat** scans every tracked .md for line counts >`LARGE_DOC_LINES = 300`; renamed constant from `LARGE_OPS_DOC_LINES`. **audit_gaps** gains universal scans for TBD/TODO/FIXME markers in tracked .md files (with skip-list for files that *describe* the marker convention rather than *use* it as a live gap) and for `build_plan/*.md` chunks not yet referenced by any closed session's archive. Plus: `BUILD_PLAN_DIR` and `PRODUCT_DOCS_DIR` module-level constants added; the test fixture monkeypatches both so tests don't scan the real repo. The universal-scan rewrite caught the audit's own scope-too-narrow failure mode (the original opt-in scope let `prep-paideia-prompt-pack.md` go undetected for 24 sessions).
- [`engine/tools/test_health_check.py`](tools/test_health_check.py) ŌĆö **fixture monkeypatch added for `BUILD_PLAN_DIR` and `PRODUCT_DOCS_DIR`** (so universal scans don't hit the real repo from the synthetic-repo tests); **two test wording updates** (`no inbound citations` ŌåÆ `zero inbound citations` matching the rewritten message text). 188 tests pass; ruff + mypy --strict clean.
- **First `lesson`-tagged MemPalace drawer captured** at the S-0041 close per the same-session convention amendment. Subject: the AI-deferral lapse this audit surfaced and the user pushed back on; the failed approach + non-obvious reason + working fix become recoverable for future sessions per the convention's structural shape. `wing: paideia, room: lessons, drawer_id: drawer_paideia_lessons_1d6c3631798c29f60c7153fa`.

### Added (S-0039 ŌĆö Structural-reference parser tool + ADR 0047)
- [`engine/adr/0047-structural-reference-parser-tool-and-adversarial-triage-workflow.md`](adr/0047-structural-reference-parser-tool-and-adversarial-triage-workflow.md) ŌĆö **new engine ADR.** Settles four operational decisions for consuming the structural-reference class established by [ADR 0046](../product/adr/0046-structural-reference-posture-extends-to-philosophy-reference-works.md): (1) the parser is a standing engine tool decoupled from phases, runnable ad-hoc whenever a source is acquired; (2) it is document-agnostic with per-document-type heuristic configs (one parser, multiple input adapters sharing a structural-detector layer; configs name document type, not source); (3) output is signal-not-truth, ephemeral-not-persisted (recall-prioritized, LLM parametric knowledge as the credibility threshold, no `engine/parser_findings/` directory, no cross-source corroboration mechanism ŌĆö reversibility named); (4) triage is adversarial, defaulting to rejection (three rejection filters: not in parametric knowledge, duplicates existing graph node, out-of-scope per [ADR 0001](../product/adr/0001-pedagogical-edges-not-historical.md)). Triage prompt template deferred to first-real-use. PDF input adapter deferred to first-PDF-source-acquisition. ADR 0046, ADR 0011, Generative Graph Independence all unchanged.
- `engine/tools/parse_structural_reference.py` ŌĆö **new module.** Standing engine tool implementing ADR 0047. Module-top contract block enumerating responsibility families and non-responsibilities; pure-function structural detectors (`detect_entries`, `detect_cross_references`, `detect_section_path`, `detect_word_count`); `InputAdapter` interface with concrete `HTMLInputAdapter` for SEP-shaped HTML (entry boundary via `<title>` + first `<h1>`; cross-references via `<a>` matching `entries/[a-z-]+/?`; section path from TOC ancestry); `FocusingBriefEmitter` producing per-entry JSON with title, id, cross-references, section-path, word-count, page-or-url, extraction-confidence; per-document-type configs (`ENCYCLOPEDIA_CONFIG`); CLI dispatch via argparse (`--source`, `--document-type`, `--output`). Mirrors the architectural shape of [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py).
- `engine/tools/test_parse_structural_reference.py` ŌĆö **new test suite.** One test class per detector (one test per logical branch), per adapter (happy-path + malformed-input), per emitter (schema correctness + confidence-score), plus integration tests against the SEP test fixtures and CLI tests via subprocess. Inherits the autouse `_scrub_git_env` fixture from [`engine/tools/conftest.py`](tools/conftest.py) per [ADR 0045](adr/0045-shared-state-integrity-discipline.md).
- `engine/tools/test_fixtures/sep/` ŌĆö **new directory** holding 5ŌĆō10 cached SEP entries' raw HTML acquired under SEP's explicit crawl-for-indexing permission per [`product/docs/content-strategy.md`](../product/docs/content-strategy.md) Tier 4. Topical diversity for cross-domain coverage testing. Parser-implementation-internal ŌĆö never reach the production graph or any user-facing surface; ADR 0011 unchanged.
- `engine/tools/requirements.txt` ŌĆö `beautifulsoup4>=4.12.0` added for the HTML input adapter. Future PDF adapter will add `pypdf` or `pdfplumber` at the session that lands it.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) ŌĆö **index entry added** for ADR 0047. Header count corrected from stale "11 ADRs total" (table already had 12) to "13 ADRs total ŌĆö all Accepted." Full-collection count updated 44 ŌåÆ 47 (13 engine + 34 product).

### Added (S-0036 ŌĆö Bash 3.2 fix + deferral-discipline guardrails)
- [`engine/tools/audit_handoff_dispositions.py`](tools/audit_handoff_dispositions.py) ŌĆö **new audit script.** Diffs `HANDOFF.md` across this session's range (`<eager-claim-SHA>^..HEAD`) and finds every newly-added section header. Each must carry a `**Disposition:**` line in one of four forms: `fixed-in-session @ <SHA>`, `deferred-with-user-confirmation`, `out-of-scope`, `not-actionable`. Hard-fails at exit 2 if any new section is missing or has a malformed disposition. Wired into the pre-commit hook for `closing` mode so the close commit cannot land if any new HANDOFF section is undispositioned. Catches the deferral pattern named in CLAUDE.md "Default to fix-in-context."
- [`engine/tools/test_audit_handoff_dispositions.py`](tools/test_audit_handoff_dispositions.py) ŌĆö **new test suite.** 29 tests covering `is_valid_disposition` (8 tests across all four valid forms + rejection cases including bare `fixed-in-session` without SHA and trailing prose after a known form), `_extract_disposition` (4 tests including first-match-wins and whitespace-stripping), `parse_added_sections` (7 tests covering empty diff, no-section diffs, single sections with/without disposition, multiple sections, edits to existing sections, and skipped diff metadata), `find_undispositioned_sections` (4 tests), plus 6 main()-integration tests via tmp_path git repos asserting exit codes 0/2 and stderr content for valid / missing-disposition / unrecognized-disposition / list-mode / existing-section-edit / no-eager-claim cases. ruff-format clean; mypy --strict clean.

### Changed (S-0036)
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) ŌĆö **persistent-warn aggregation refactored from associative arrays (bash 4+) to parallel indexed arrays (bash 3.2 portable).** The prior code used `declare -A CATEGORY_FIRINGS` and `${!CATEGORY_FIRINGS[@]}` for key iteration ŌĆö both bash 4+ features. macOS ships `/bin/bash` 3.2; the shebang resolves to that, so the persistent-warn surface had been silently emitting "none above the 3-of-5 threshold" regardless of archive contents (today invisible because all recent archives carry zero soft-warns; would have suppressed real persistence detection). Replaced with parallel `CATEGORY_NAMES` + `CATEGORY_FIRINGS` indexed arrays plus a `_find_category_index` helper using a C-style for-loop. Verified on `bash 3.2.57` ŌĆö hook runs clean, no `declare: -A: invalid option` error. The HANDOFF.md S-0035 entry queuing this fix is removed (resolved). Side discovery surfaced at S-0035 close; the original deferral was retroactively the wrong call per the new "Default to fix-in-context" posture rule.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) ŌĆö **new "Default to fix-in-context" posture rule** under standing rules. Codifies that a bug found mid-session whose fix is in context defaults to inline fix; deferral requires user confirmation OR a named threshold (substantial scope / contract change / budget cap reached). Mechanically backstopped by the new disposition audit. No ADR per user direction at S-0036 ŌĆö the contract layer stays light; CLAUDE.md is the load-bearing surface for session-internal posture rules.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) ŌĆö **new closing-mode hard-fail block** invokes `audit_handoff_dispositions.py`. The close commit cannot land if any new HANDOFF.md section in the session lacks a valid disposition. Mirrors the gate-stack pattern (validate.py default + --code-gates + --sql-gates).
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) ŌĆö **new step 6a "HANDOFF-disposition audit"** documents the audit, the four accepted disposition forms, and the resolution path (apply the fix in this session and use `fixed-in-session @ <SHA>`, OR get user confirmation and use `deferred-with-user-confirmation`). Notes that the audit also fires from pre-commit closing-mode so manual invocation is a way to catch issues before staging.
- [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) ŌĆö **mirror of step 6a** per ADR 0036/0044 doc ŌåÆ skill propagation discipline.
- [`HANDOFF.md`](../HANDOFF.md) ŌĆö **bash 3.2 entry deleted** (resolved at S-0036 by the session-start.sh refactor).

### Added (S-0035 ŌĆö Engine hardening for restart: subprocess env scrub + atomic mempalace + boot-time probes)
- [`engine/adr/0045-shared-state-integrity-discipline.md`](adr/0045-shared-state-integrity-discipline.md) ŌĆö **new ADR (engine).** Mechanizes four shared-state integrity rules in response to S-0033 (env-leak wrote `core.bare=true` to parent `.git/config`) and S-0034 (chromadb HNSW segment corruption crashed every subsequent session). Subprocess env scrubbing across all hooks + `validate.py`'s 4 code-gate subprocess calls; atomic `cp -a` snapshot + `probe_palace.py` verify + rollback wrapper around `mempalace hook run`; boot-time `validate.py --health-probe-only` invoked from `session-start.sh`; shutdown soft-warn aggregation changes from "final validator run only" to "max-count across all this-session `validate-history.jsonl` invocations" so boot-only probe firings reach the archive. Default-mode validator check count rises 14 ŌåÆ 16.
- [`engine/tools/scrub_env.py`](tools/scrub_env.py) ŌĆö **new helper.** `scrubbed_env(base=None)` returns a copy of an env dict with every `GIT_*` key removed; `scrub_in_place(env)` mutates in place. Used by `validate.py` for subprocess `env=` parameter and by `probe_repo.py` for its own git subprocess calls.
- [`engine/tools/scrub_env.sh`](tools/scrub_env.sh) ŌĆö **new bash helper.** Defines `scrub_git_env` function that unsets every `GIT_*` variable in the current shell. Sourced by all four hook scripts before they shell out. Portable across bash 3.2 and bash 4+.
- [`engine/tools/conftest.py`](tools/conftest.py) ŌĆö **new pytest config.** Hoists the `_scrub_git_env` autouse fixture from `test_audit_side_discoveries.py` so the GIT_* env scrub applies to every test in the suite, not just the side-discovery tests. The original fixture remains in place ŌĆö both running is idempotent.
- [`engine/tools/probe_palace.py`](tools/probe_palace.py) ŌĆö **new probe script.** Opens chromadb `PersistentClient` at `~/.mempalace/palace`, lists collections, calls `get_collection() + count()` on each. Sub-second on a 130 MB palace. Exit codes: 0 healthy, 1 suspect, 2 hard-broken; SIGSEGV (139) is treated as hard-broken by callers ŌĆö the S-0034 chromadb_rust_bindings signature. `MEMPALACE_PROBE_PALACE_PATH` env var override exists for testing.
- [`engine/tools/probe_repo.py`](tools/probe_repo.py) ŌĆö **new probe script.** Checks worktree's effective `core.bare`, parent clone's standalone `.git/config` `core.bare` (catches the S-0033 worktree-override-masks-broken-parent case), HEAD resolution. Same exit-code convention as `probe_palace.py`.
- [`engine/tools/test_scrub_env.py`](tools/test_scrub_env.py) ŌĆö **new test suite.** 11 tests covering both `scrubbed_env` and `scrub_in_place`: GIT_* removal, non-GIT preservation, source-dict immutability, explicit-base parameter, empty-dict handling, return-self-for-chaining.
- [`engine/tools/test_probe_palace.py`](tools/test_probe_palace.py) ŌĆö **new test suite.** 4 tests: missing palace dir ŌåÆ suspect; empty palace dir ŌåÆ suspect or hard-broken; healthy palace via real chromadb ŌåÆ exit 0; findings emit on stderr.
- [`engine/tools/test_probe_repo.py`](tools/test_probe_repo.py) ŌĆö **new test suite.** 5 tests: clean repo ŌåÆ exit 0; `core.bare=true` ŌåÆ exit 2 with hard-broken message; outside git repo ŌåÆ exit 2; findings emit on stderr; recovery message names correct path.

### Changed (S-0035)
- [`engine/tools/validate.py`](tools/validate.py) ŌĆö **subprocess env scrubbing on all 4 code-gate calls** (ruff check, ruff format, mypy --strict, pytest at lines ~820, 830, 840, 873) ŌĆö pass `env=scrubbed_env()`. **New `validate_shared_state_health()`** dispatches `probe_palace.py` and `probe_repo.py` as subprocesses, mapping exit codes 0/1/2/139 to `add_check` / `soft_warn` / `hard_fail`. Wired into the default check set so every pre-commit run includes shared-state checks. **New `--health-probe-only` flag** dispatches only the shared-state checks for the SessionStart hook's sub-second boot-time verification. **conftest.py exempted from test-presence rule** so it doesn't trigger a false-positive "no test file for conftest.py" hard-fail.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/session-start.sh`](tools/hooks/session-start.sh) ŌĆö **shared-state health probe step added** between cadence trigger and persistent-warn surface. Runs `validate.py --health-probe-only`; surfaces healthy as one-liner, soft-warn as stderr block citing categories, hard-broken as a LOUD attention banner pointing at ADR 0045 for diagnostics. Hook still always exits 0 (a hard-broken state must remain diagnosable from within a session). **Sources `scrub_env.sh`** at the top so `git rev-parse --show-toplevel` runs against a clean env.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/post-state-edit.sh`](tools/hooks/post-state-edit.sh), [`engine/tools/hooks/post-adr-write.sh`](tools/hooks/post-adr-write.sh) ŌĆö **source `scrub_env.sh` and call `scrub_git_env`** before their `git rev-parse --show-toplevel` calls (and `mempalace search` in the ADR-write hook). Defense-in-depth against future leaked `GIT_DIR` from any sub-agent or Skill context.
- [`engine/tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh`](tools/hooks/mempalace-hook-wrapper.sh) ŌĆö **atomic-write wrapper around `mempalace hook run`.** Pre-mine `cp -a` snapshot to `palace.pre-mine` plus parallel KG snapshot dir; invoke mempalace with scrubbed env; post-mine `probe_palace.py` verify; on healthy/suspect rotate snapshot to `palace.last-good` (one retained between hook fires); on hard-broken or SIGSEGV roll back palace + KG and force the hook's eventual EXIT_CODE non-zero so the next session's boot reading of `mempalace-hook.log` surfaces the rollback event. Snapshot semantics are byte-level (`cp -a`); minor inconsistency window from mid-WAL-write at snapshot time accepted because corruption recovery dwarfs that cost.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) ŌĆö **step 8 amended** for the soft-warn aggregation change per ADR 0045 Decision 4: compute `outcome_summary_soft_warns` by max-count aggregation across every `validate.py` invocation in this session's `validate-history.jsonl` entries, not just the final pre-commit run. Schema example gains `chromadb_palace_health` and `repo_config_health` keys. Aggregation procedure spelled out (filter by session_id or timestamp window; per-category max).
- [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) ŌĆö **mirror of the step 8 amendment** per ADR 0036/0044 doc ŌåÆ skill propagation discipline.
- [`engine/operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md`](operations/tools-validate-interpretation.md) ŌĆö **two new soft-warn category entries** (`chromadb_palace_health`, `repo_config_health`) under "Soft-warns (signal, not blocker)" with recovery procedures. The hard-fail escalation (definite corruption blocks the commit) is documented inline so the suspicion / hard-broken split is clear.
- [`CLAUDE.md`](../CLAUDE.md) ŌĆö **Posture vs machinery section narrows further** with three new mechanized rules (subprocess env scrubbing, mempalace atomic-write, boot-time shared-state probes) per ADR 0045.
- [`engine/adr/README.md`](adr/README.md) ŌĆö index entry added for ADR 0045.
- [`engine/STATE.md`](STATE.md) ŌĆö Current phase row appended with S-0035 close summary; Last build session row ŌåÆ S-0035 (engine hardening); Prior build session row ŌåÆ S-0034 (rolls in); Next session work item ŌåÆ S-0036 = Phase 4 graph validation (the work originally planned for S-0035, displaced by this hardening session). ### Added (S-0033 ŌĆö Pre-commit STATUS-capture bug + side-discovery audit + scheduling-barrier fix)
- [`engine/tools/audit_side_discoveries.py`](tools/audit_side_discoveries.py) ŌĆö **new tool** per [HANDOFF.md](../HANDOFF.md) Item 2. Session-shutdown audit gate that requires explicit disposition for follow-up markers in commit messages. Scans this session's commit-message text (range `<eager-claim-SHA>..HEAD`) for case-insensitive whole-word matches against `flagged`, `follow-up`, `follow up`, `TODO`, `FIXME`, `deferred`, `noted for`, `future session`, `next session`, `pending`, `out of scope`. Filters obvious negations preceded by `no` / `not` / `nothing` / `no longer` within ~12 chars. Matches each hit against the `side_discoveries` field in `engine/session/current.json`; exit 2 (hard-fail) on undispositioned markers, exit 0 if all matched or none found. CLI: `--range`, `--dispositions`, `--list` (dry-run). Layer 1 contract docstring per ADR 0038 + ADR 0039.
- [`engine/tools/test_audit_side_discoveries.py`](tools/test_audit_side_discoveries.py) ŌĆö **new test suite** ŌĆö 22 tests covering scan_markers (basic hit, case-insensitive, negation filter, distinct-phrases-in-one-commit, hyphenated vs spaced follow-up, context newline stripping), is_negated, match_dispositions (pairing by sha-prefix + marker, undispositioned-only, extra-dispositions ignored), load_dispositions (missing file, no field, marker normalization, non-list rejection), and main() integration via tmp_path git fixtures (no markers, undispositioned, all dispositioned, --list flag, --range override) plus find_eager_claim_sha and session_range. ruff-format clean; mypy --strict clean.

### Changed (S-0033)
- [`engine/tools/hooks/pre-commit`](tools/hooks/pre-commit) ŌĆö **STATUS=$? capture bug fix** per HANDOFF.md Item 1. The three `if ! cmd; then STATUS=$?; ...` blocks (validate.py, --code-gates, --sql-gates) had been silently allowing hard-fails through because `$?` after a negated pipeline always evaluates to 0 (the negation's success). Replaced each block with the `STATUS=0; cmd || STATUS=$?` pattern, which preserves `set -e` semantics and captures cmd's actual exit code. Verified by smoke-test: a deliberate mypy --strict violation now blocks the commit (exit 1) where previously it was silently accepted. Also: **`engine/scheduled_audits.json` added to exploration-mode allowed-paths** per HANDOFF.md Item 3 ŌĆö scheduling a near-term audit between sessions no longer requires opening a session. The hook docstring header is updated to list the new allowed path.
- [`engine/operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md`](operations/session-shutdown-sequence.md) ŌĆö **new step 6 "Side-discovery audit"** inserted between ENGINE_LOG (step 5) and diary (renumbered to step 7) per HANDOFF.md Item 2. Hard-fail gate; the script does not introduce a new soft-warn category. Steps 7ŌåÆ8, 8ŌåÆ9, 9ŌåÆ10 renumbered; Recovery section step references updated; internal cross-references in steps 7/8 updated to point at the new step numbering.
- [`.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md`](../.claude/skills/session-shutdown-sequence/SKILL.md) ŌĆö **mirror of the new step 6** per ADR 0036/0044 doc ŌåÆ skill propagation discipline. Pre-existing Recovery-section step-number drift (steps 1ŌĆō8 / step 7 / step 8 references that were already stale against the ops doc's 9-step numbering) corrected in passing.
